yella yeṭṭef addud mgal yugurten deg yimenɣiyen gar igelliden yufa d iman is yessefk ad yerwel seg tmurt is deffir tiẓẓegzent n qiṛta d tmenɣiwt n ɛeẓrabeɛl yessenza t simbrunyus i yesmersen taqunsult ɣer tama n kantus minikyus
rufus deffir bistya issenza t ihi iwakken ad i d ssekkrent ifaṛes asurdu d rrebrab tinnɣuwin n yugurten iwakken ad d yessuter deg useqqamu n yemɣaren ad kazen yes d agellid ɣef numidya
imi d yefruri seg uẓar n massinisa di tuga i wselḥu n imenɣi yesmenyif uqensul as yesseqdec yalec wala ad yeǧǧ tiɣawsiwin rekdent tamnaḍt n numidya d netta ay d tṣaḥma d meqdunya d minikyus i d saḥ simi yebda msiwa anadi s iḥulfa yugurten belli yuɣal ur yezmir ara ad yettkel ɣef yemdukal is kra deg sen kukran kra nniḍen ugaden afḍaḥ neɣ tafgurt yugurten ihi yesmagel ikellef bunilkan ukkud yesɛa taflest ɣef wuffiren is i yellan d imiḍwel yesmagel it ad yesseqdec s tedrimt am akken yennum wid ara yenɣen missiwa s tuffra neɣ akken twuta tegnitt isled bumilkaṛ s lemɣawla assusel n ugellid ifern d kra n yemdanen i ytewlen di tɣawsiwin am tigi
gganin amussu n missiwa d idaɣaren uɣur yettṛuḥu d wakkud n tuffɣa ines
gan as akmin anda iwuta
immeɣ yiwen deg sen ɣef missiwa ixettet it yenɣa t maca ur iḥezzeb ara akken iwuta yettwaṭṭef iferreh d imi tḥeṛsen aṭas n medden ladɣa aqenṣul albinus
ma d bumilkar i d yedduklen netta d wergaz ɣer ṛuma seddaw usenkid n uwanek aṛumani yettwaḍfer ccil aṣaḍuf agmawi acku taɣdemt d tugedd ssefken ayenni ma d ayen yerzan yugurten ɣas ulamma tettwasentem tmenɣiwt yugi ad ikaz yeṭṭef deg ukuddel alammi yeẓra belli tazrirt d yedrimen ines tɛedda nnig sen tinnɣi tanessaraft yeḍṛan imir nni ɣas yeka d asenkid smusett n yemddukal is di tbeddit tamezwarut zdat teɣdemt
yesban d belli d ajaxfafa kan i t iceɣben mačči d igad isersen iman nsen d asenkid
yuzen bumelkar s tuffra ɣer numidya yugad ad ẓer ffɣen lɣaci ɣef tulelt ines imi ẓran yiwen deg imallalen ines yettwafka ɣer udagaẓ iṛuḥ ula d netta deffir n kra bbussan imi as yessawel useqqamu n yemɣaren iwakken ad yeffeɣ di italya
imi yeffeɣ di ṛuma ɣef akken d nnan yezzi tamuɣli s aṭas n tikal lewhi n ṛuma s tsusmi taggara isuɣ yenna tamdint i tmenziwt ur tettɛeṭṭil ara ad tehtuti ma tufa wara tt yaɣen ineyyer imenɣi ihi yuzzel albinus ɣer waggay n lḥerǧ d tiɣraḍ d kra yellan yesdulli i yiserdasen n friqya
am akken tedda tnamit deffir mara teḍru testant tamezwarut d usenṭeq n inigan yessefk ɣef umedu ad yefk asenkid ara yḍemnen tihawt ines deg ibeddi ara d iḍefren
yerna iṛuḥ ula d netta iḥar ad ifak imenɣi agi s yiɣil d yemrigen neɣ s tuṭṭfa n yugurten neɣ s webrid nniḍen zzat tefranin ur tettɛeṭṭil ara ad d tilint s wegmaḍ ɣer wayagi yella yugurten yesmezgir yesnulfuy d isemmezgiren nniḍen imaynuten war arkad yettṛeggim s wannuz tikwal tikwal nniḍen ad isured ireggimen ɣef zzeḍmat u tikwal d netta i yẓeddmen iwakken ur feččlen ara imeḍfaren ines s tewzel yesmeɛlik s uqenṣul s uzemmezger s temlellit gar imenɣi d tifrat kra ikcem iten ccek
llan ula d wid yurdan belli aneggaru agi yezga s uɣawas n ugellid u daɣen asemmezger agi deg temhilin deffir beddu amɣiwel yusa d d aselkan neɣ d agmuḍ n tkerrast ugar n wegmuḍ n tewzizt aɛgaz akken yebɣu yili akud yella yagi yezri ass n tefranin yuẓ d albinus yeǧǧa gma s ulus deg wegrur am d abru briṭuṛ u netta yekkunser ɣer ṛuma
di ṛuma imir nni tella tegduda tcerreg s wudem yessagaden s tmentelt n tnekra i d smessen igensasen n yella yessefk ɣef uqensul ad yenbeḍ tifranin wideg ara d ffɣen iqensulen n useggas ara d ḍefṛen u llan iqensulen ttaddamen tawuri nsen deg umenzu n yennayer tifranin derrunt s tuddsa deg wezgen useggas s imisi maca tikwal tettgellilayagi yeḍra d di tallit n uqenṣul albinus
d anawur afellay netta s umata d abrutur i yella yagi yettwasmiggel i wenbaḍ n tenbaḍt ttwafkant as yall tinbaḍin igensasen deg sen weɣref
sin bibilyus d likyus anyusttnadin ad sɣezzfen tizziwt nsen ccil imidawen nsen amqelleɛ agi yeswaɣ tifranin i teɣzi useggas
amzizger agi isegger ulyus yeǧǧan anbaḍ n yigen am akken i d nenna yagi s taggayt is bru britur isegger it ad irmi ad iɛreḍ asebded n imebnɣi neɣ asukkes n tedrimt seg ugellid s usagged is s imenɣi yessuffeɣ d tarbaɛt is deg wagur n yennayer iwakken ad yeg zzeḍma s tikli izerben ccil tasemhuyt tuqjiṛt
yewweḍ ɣer temdint sutul anda tella tesbaynut tageldant
anda tella tesbaynutt tageldant yir tignewt d yideg n temdint ur as ssurufen ara iwakken ad tt yekcem wala ad tt yessutel acku i tuɣzi n igadiren yettwaksan ɣef yiri n wedrar aḥecṛaṛaf tezzi yas d luḍa yeččuren d aluḍ u yerra tt ugeffur d alma n waluḍ ɣas akken am d aɣussu i yebɣa iwakken ad yessiged agellid
am akken d tidet nezzeh yettbeggin aɣ d belli tifranin ur d ḍrint ara aseggas dat sɛ ɣef wayagi i d yuɣal albinyus ɣer ifriqya s twuri ines d abruqunsul i useggas agi
u yessefk ad yettwafren mitilus i useggas ara d iḍefren ayagi mgal wid i d yeqqaren belli mitilus yettwasmel d aqusul i useggas dat sɛ
ɣef usentel agi
wali muḥemmed lhadi ḥarec
aṭṭaṭawwur assiyyasi wal iqṭisadi fi numidya mundu ɛtilaa massinisa lɛarc ila wafat yuba al awwal qabla el milad
risalt majister
jamiɛet el djazayer
tasegrest tasegresst n iserdasen d igruren i deg sɛeddayen tasemhuyt n tegrest
yennayer dat sɛ
sutul d tamdint n galma n wass a deg usamer azdayri
iwakken ad yesgunfu isegger it lebɣi n ukeččumn temdint d uḥelli n tesbaynut ihegga d akk allalen yeṣka tarsal d ilukta isseḥres ɣef iweẓla yak iwutan ad smersen aɣawas is
yegza yugurten s uheggi n unebbaḍ am akken yegza s tumumt ines
yessebɣes it s tiddenkit deg leḥmeq ines ad as yanez tiggensest deffir tayeḍ yessuter taflast netta yesteɛmil ireggel yessedduy igen ines ger tẓegwa d iberdan iwezzlanen taggara issenẓa t s usirem n tifrat s wemsefrek uffir s tukksa n usutel ɣef sutul d weqḍaɛ is temnaḍin yeṭṭurfan am akken yeṭṭafeṛ it deg deg uwexxeṛ is
s wakken nni ad yili ubekkaḍ is yeffer ugar yuɣ lḥal yezga yettnadi deg yiḍ deg wass s yergazen at inabbaḍen n tmiḍi d tarmit isertayen ifesyanen
yessenẓay kra ad rewlen ɣur s kra s tuǧǧit n wammassen sen lawan n wesɣal licaṛa
imi yedda yalec akken i t yesseɣwes d wakken yebɣa s teẓwayt yassutel agrur n ulus s waṭas n inumidiyen
azdam agi s lɣila issebheḍ iserdasen iṛumaniyen kra ttarnin ad srekden imaggaden tugdin d unezgum ɛeddan tilas amguggi n icenga tallest n yiḍ tebrek igenni s isigna rran amihi yessaɣen ɣef yal tamiwin ugar
medden akk dinna ttekkin deg usemɣer n herrwel d tsemessit
ur zmiren ara ad ɣetsen ma yessefk ad rewlen neɣ ad qqimen
gar tɣalmin tirebbuyaɛ yettwasguffsen am akken i d nebder yakan s liquṛya d tsiritin traqitin d kra iserdasen imaynuten i yrewlen ɣer wedrar n ugellid di tegnitt nni dɣa aɣella wis amidan n taggayt tamezwarut n terbaɛt tis kraḍ yelli asaka i ucengu di tlemmast n uḥfir i ɣef yrttwaseɣlef ad yemmestan fell as u syinna i d kecmen inumidiyen s tdusi lqewwa
rewlen iserdasen nneɣ tugett deg sen ḍeggṛen imrigen nsen ṛuḥen ɣer yiwet n tewrirt d yuẓen
yeɣli d yiḍ yettwaḥweṣ wegrur agi yessebɣes acengu ad idegger tarennawt alamma d iri s
azekka nni yeḍṛa wemsawel gar yugurten d ulus ulamma yella yessutel igen is u yella yezmer ad t issenger s wuzzal d laẓ ɣas akken ihi rnu arekki lemqadṛa n tḍermist n tlumist tamadant yebɣa ad yemqacaḥ d ulus u ad yessuref fell as meṛṛa deffir ma ara ten yesɛeddi s ddaw uzaglu
u s tewtilt ara ten yessufɣen di numidya di tlemmast n temrawt n wussan
acḥal i qqejrent acḥal i sseklalent tewtilin am tigi imi d yufa iman is ur yesɛi ara afran ḥala ad ideggi neɣ ad immet
ihi yeḍṛa d wemtawa akken i t yebɣa ugellid
imi ttwasussnent tedyenin agi di ṛuma yeɣli d lxulɛa
kra ttrun ɣef wannar n fell as unezgum d umerkud kra ur ssinen ara iweẓla n imenɣan ugaden ɣef tlelli nsen meṛṛa rfan feqɛen ɣef ulus ladɣa wid nni yettwassnen aṭas n tikwal s tebɣest nsen di taɣult n imenɣi u ẓeran d akken ur ssurufen ara madden i wḍella anebbaḍ aserdas yettnadin ɣef lemneɛ deg ixxiṭṭ lɛaṛ yal ager iɣallaten n tmiḍi n tsertutin d aɣella n tmiḍi n taggayt tamezwarut
yella yesɛa azal ugar aɣella amiḍan n taggayt tis snat
asegzi n wayenni ad t naf ɣur flurus
imrigen gar ifassen is
s wakka i yugad uqensul albinus ad d yeglu wagul i yesker gma s s wurfan n wegdud fell as netta ibda yessesmun tazemmalt deffir mi d yessenked taɣawsa n ugatu yga ɣef useqqamu n yemɣaren u yessuter ulus ma d tidet tallalt deg yemsisen d wegdud alatini
iberreḥ d useqqamu n yemɣaren u yella yesɛa tiɣẓint belli d awezɣi ad naru kra n ugatu mebla ma yeɣtes useqqamu n yemɣaren yak d wegdud aṛumani deffir mi yegdel s wegmaḍ seg igensasen n wegdud amata tiddukla d yigen i d yessers i d yesserdesyekkunsel uqensul ɣer ifriqya acku igen aṛumani yak akken d inna wemtawa yesɛedda tagrest di temnaḍt taṛumanit
yella yebɣa nezzeh ad yeḍfer bih bih yugurten u ad isfeḍ ixiṭṭ lɛaṛ n gma s imi yeẓṛa anafag n yigen ines yuder rnu ɣer wayagi tarenbaḍt abuder ahegges i d yekkan di war aɣyud iɣtes ur ittarmi acemma imir nni
xl di tegnitt nni di ruma isres d uqensul n uɣaref kayus manilus limitanus zdat wegdud asenfar n uṣaḍuf iswi ines d tullya n testant mgal wigad nni yessbeɣsen yugurten ad yelku ad yeḥqeṛ tiɣtasin n useqqamu n yemɣaren u mgal wid nni i yeṭṭfen adrim lawan deg aydeg ttwaɣelfen s tiggensest d tinbaḍin yak d widak nni i as yerran ilwan d iserdasen imerwal
di taggara widak nni yellan d yitliṭen n ucengu deg wayen yerzan tammazalt d imenɣi
asumer agi i yesnuɣnin aṭas n medden kra gzan belli llan d ibekkaḍen wiyeḍnin ugaden ad ilin d tiɣtasin n ukasan n wegdud maca llan ur zmiren ara ad sgemden ɛinani bla ma kazen belli ɣetsen agulen i deg d iwwet d wiyeḍnin yettemyaken anzi sqedcen imeddukal nsen ladɣa llati d yemsisen sen i wesnulfu n yal iswaɣ yellumẓen maca yuɛeṛ ɣef wemdan ad issugen d acu n unafag d tewast i yes yefren wegdud ɣef issumren
macci s teɣdeft i tebɣurin n tegduda maca s ukasan i yheggaren i yettjeddiren deg s s ugella
ɣer dagi i tewweḍ tdewwast n ikabaren imir nni
di tegnitt deg aydeg llan iheggaren xullɛen markus skawrus amarag n bistya zik nni ifuṛes tagnitt am akken i d nenna yagi i deg feṛḥen medden u yexleɛ ukanar is am akken tella temdint diɣenna tenhewwal ifuṛeṣ ayagi yakk iwakken ad yesmel yiwen seg kṛaḍ imastanen yettallalen mamilya am akken d inna uṣaduf tasestant ur d telli ara mebla iwennan iqanniwen d unafag n weɣref
tikli agi n mɣaci n weɣref tefka anzi ɣer tin n iheggaren u tefṛeḥ s trennawt ines tuqbiḥt
di tillawt ur yeqqim ara d aqensul imi tiɣalafin is fukent deg n useggas iɛeddan u yella d abru qunsul alammi yettwaɛzel
wali ayen d iḍefren taseddart
d taɣtast yessufeɣ itt id ugensas n uɣref amata kayus malilyus limtanus di tazwara n useggas dat sɛ am akken yelha usali
iswi ines d asbeddi n tesmilt tuɣdimt seg yemnayen iwakken ad caṛɛen igad yak yettwardan sɛan afus d yugurten tiḥercewt u ɣemren tt takṛiḍt d tanbaḍt ssaɣen rnu ɣer wayagi tuɣal d tnamit n wemqelleɛ gar ikabaren d trebbuyaɛ d tsekrarin d teswawayent
ayagi yella iban d yagi di ṛuma di kra iseggasen yagi di lawan n tmazzalt d tenkelwit tangawit iwumi yettak wemdan tazwert
maca zdat useɣli n qerṭaǧa aseqqamu n yemɣaren yak d wegdud aṛumani bḍan tanbaḍt war arumsu wala takriḍt
la annaz taftilt n wala wemqelleɛ gar iɣermanen tugdin seg ucengu tugeẓ ɣef temdint maca deg wasmi tekkes tugdi ɣef yemdanen flalint d tbuciḍanin n leɛgez d tizzengert
icenga yezgan tteddun d tenkelwit akka i tuɣal talwit i llan ssaramen tt n lekmer tuɣal d aṭṭan yugaren lekmer s timmad is deg ass n d afella yuɣal weḥmal n tenbaḍt ɣur iheggaren d weḥmal n tlelli ɣur lɣaci n weɣref uɣalen d aḥmal imzernen imekreḍ
u d netta i ɣef ttxemmin yak medden
yuɣal wemdan iḥeggeṣ yettaker akken yebɣa yuɣal yalec yebḍa tagduda ɛzizen imir nni tettwacerreg abruy abruy
ɣas yella wayagi yak aḥulfu n temsetla yezga ɣur iheggaren yessenked asen tamanegt wegdud d nitni i d tuggti
ulamma tella tuggti agi tennezwi tebḍa tadersi d tameẓyant tella tbeṭṭu tnebbeḍ di tɣawsiwin n imenɣi d tmazzalt d tasbaynut n uwanek d timnadin d ixawiyen
ma d agdud amur ines d leqdic aserdasi yak d tigullelt d zzelṭ
ma d igelfan n imenɣi ttuɣalen i ynebbaḍen d at teglamin
di tegnit agi imawlan n iserdasen neɣ arraw nsen ma llan zedɣen ɣer tama n walbɛaḍ yellan d aneflus untim ad ten ssufɣen di tmezduɣt nsen
akka i teẓẓa tdusi tameqqrant tanaɣubt tameqqrant deg ulawen ayagi kra yessekreffet yettwaqqadaren yettwazekkayen akka alamma teɣli
tdusi agi yesɣḍel itt ubekkaḍ is
ladɣa simi d flalin kra n iheggaren yettaken afran i yiseɣ adetti ɣef weɣmar ukriḍ tengugi tmurt meṛṛa am akken iwwet urejraj tamurt u ysegger amennuɣ aɣeṛman imdanen iɣermanen
imi yebda tibiryus d kayus qarakus imenɣi nsen
aṭas n tiwalin timeqqranin i gan i tegduda di tamllit nni n imenɣiyen ibuniqen d tiyeḍnin ssuturen izerfan n wegdud ad isɛu tilelli u kecfen d kra n tinɣiwin n kra iheggaren i wmahi u ẓran ibekkaḍen nsen ssutren tallalt iwakken ad zbun i wmussu n iqarakiyen s yemsisen d llatin tikwal u tikwal nniḍen s yemnayen iwumi kellxen s uṛeggem n wemtawa yid sen
di tazwara n tafluft nɣan tibiryus seg s akkin s kra iseggasen nɣan kayus i yellan ɣef webrid n gma s
amezwaru yella d agensas n lɣaci n weɣref
wayeḍnin yella yesbedday igelfan
markus fulfyus flakus teḍra yid s kif kif
ulac din usurdu belli iqarakiyen yellan ttraǧun tarennawt ixuṣ iten umeqqin i yesfilliten iṛumaniyen inebkaḍen maca ttif tiṛẓi i bab n tirrugza wala tarennawt tukriḍt ad a tt id iḥelli ulamma ɣef tekriḍt s wallalen izernanen
akka dɣa iheggaren sqedcen tarennawt nsen di lfayda n tugumt ccehwa nsen nɣan zewwgen aṭas iɣermanen
s wakken nni swawen d i yemal ugan n imihiyan wala tadusi acku qrib ayen yesseɣlin meṛṛa iwanaken imeqqranen d lehbal n trennawt
wakken yebɣu yili wazal is d win dɣa i yesremden yal tama yak d unadi sunafag i usenger ucengu yettwarnan maca ma tebɣiḍ ameslay ɣef imennuɣen n temdint d tezrirt nsen ɣef tɣariwin n temdint ulamma asentel agi yesɛa aṭas n teɣdef i yuklal
macci d tanga kan i yettfakan akkud diɣenna
deffir temyaqqant ulus d uɣelluy ucmit n trebbuyaɛ nneɣ bdan sin mitilus yak d silanus timnaḍin
tusa d numidya d amur n mitilus d argaz urmid ɣur s ddur yettwassen mebla asurdu xas ma yella d amenzaɣ n ukabar aɣerfan
simi yeddem tizziwt yeǧǧa i wemdakel is iqensulen yettwasemlen mettelyus i wen ifkan isem unumidi ilmend n tarrayt i yes s yesselḥa imenɣi mgal yugurten yuklal asmineg n yall imarayen iqbuṛen
iṭṭef aṭas n tɣawiyin zzat ma ad yaweḍ ɣer tqenṣult aseggas dat sɛ yettwasmel d asefrak anejbar aseggas dat sɛ u d agensas n weɣrem amata aseggas u d asefrak n temdint aseggas yuɣal d aseggas dat sɛ d anebbaḍ n siqilya aseggas n sɛ
ma d silanus ad yettwarn zzeg s akkin si tam n lkambireyyin
aḥraz n wayen nniḍen yakk
yefka iman is yak i wḥerkel i imenɣi ara yesselḥu netta yurda igen amenzu
ismun tazemmalt tirebbuyaɛ
yewwi d yal tamiwin tiɣlamin timaragin issegrew d imrigen n ẓẓedma d wid n tmastant igmar d yal ayen ara ynefɛen imenɣi bu waddaden imattayen ɣur sen aṭas n tɣawsiwin
rnu ɣer wayagi ismal it useqqamu n yemɣaren lawan n uḥerkal agi d tenbaḍt ines imi yekfa uheggi d usuddes n yalec am akken yebɣa iṛuḥ ɣer numidya yewwi yid s taflest iɣermanen ines taflest ur nesɛi tilas deg tehdi ines imi macci d win ara yettwasgufsen
di tillawt tajlaq i yeṛẓan tadusi nneɣ di numidya alammi d ass a u yeslal tadusi n ucengu nneɣ
imi yewweḍ ɣer ifriqya iṭṭef d s ɣur sebrunyus albinus igen d anamun yeḍɛef ur yezmir ad yeg ussis neɣ ad ilawi imihiyen
d ameslay iwumi yezmer ugar tigawt iheggeṣ imisan nneɣ ihegges d seg ucengu bla tuddsa wala aḍebber
amumi agi n wantum yellan di trebbuyaɛ n yigen amaynut u yeswawi yas d anezgum yugaren asirem i as d ittak umaḍan nsen
ɣas akken ccil azemmezger n tefranin d isnekẓen deg wakud yesɛa ifassen is ad yessuddes tamḍugt ẓẓedma u netta dagi yessentem aɣ s salustyus ayen i d nenna yagi
asebter uṭun utun belli albinus yuɣal d ɣer ifriqya s yisem is d brunqunṣul aseggas n dat sɛ
yeẓra acḥal ara ttganin iɣermanen agmuḍ n tedyanin d ineḍruyen
ɣas akken yeɣtes mitilus ur ibeddu ara imenɣi skud ur unzen ara iserdasen i wuddus aqbuṛ acku alyus iwumi yumen waqqas deffir mi yečča tiɣrit tiṛẓi gma s ulus iɣtes ur iteffeɣ ara di tlisa n temnaḍt u yeǧǧa iserdasen ka yekka unebdu deg yegruren yeẓẓan ur yesmuttuy ara idigan is
igruren agi iserdasen ur sɛin ara igadiren wala tiɛessasin am wakken tt isdulli wuddus aserdas
yal yiwen yettaǧǧa amḍiq is mi as yehwa
iqeddacen keččmen ɣur iserdasen ttmenḍaren deg yiḍ deg wass
u deg umender agi ssekrifiten igran urtiyen ttkewwicen leḥwac leɛzuyab s yiɣil ttkewwicen actal d waklan ssenfalen ten d yemzenza s ccrab d tangiwin n wučči n taggayt agi
rnu ɣer wayagi znuzuyen irden i asen yettak uwanek u ttajjawen d aɣrum yal ass
s tzwzel yal tiwaɣiyin d ittekken di leɛgez d ubekkaḍ d uheggeṣ
aɛgaz d ubekkaḍ d uhegges i nezmer ad d nini ad nessugen belli llant yak deg yigen agi u yella wayen nniḍen
deg wemlasay ines mgal iswaɣen agi ttwaliɣ mitilus yesseflali d diɣenna timmuqṛa d tnuẓiẓt
am akken yella way agi diɣenna d tiggayin tiserdasi ines
yeẓra amek ara yeḥrez amuzzu anaruz d talmamt tumzidt
yebda s yissir n kra d iswawayen lefcal s usegdel n tnezzutn ccṛab yak d yal učči yewwan deg sen imusden d iserdasen d yat n wedrur aserdasi
u yegdel ɣef iqeddacen ad ddun d iserdasen tirebbuyaɛ imagnuten akken yegdel tiddin taɣin n leḥwayec n waggay neɣ n waklan u yegdel aɣcad nniḍen s tseddit
nnig wayagi yella yessmuttuy yal ass agrur ɣef iberdan ugzimen iferg iten s igadiren itezzi yas d s yeḥfiren amzun acengu ara d iteddu
yesbedday imḍafen di yal ansa amḍiq iteffeɣ netta s timmad is yettgiwis iten
yessefqad teddun ifesyanen ines
akken diɣenna lawan n tikli ad tafeḍ tikwal ɣer zzat tikwal ɣer deffir
iḥeṛṛes iwakken yiwen ur iteffeɣ ɣef udar u ad lḥun d aserbub idis n ikenyalen
u yal aserdas ad yawi imreg d lmuna iman is
s wakka i yesgugg agulen mebla asurdu fell asent iman unnig i yigen ines
di tegnitt nni dɣa idall yugurten s iɣellaten ines ɣef wermud n mitilus ayɣef d yewwi isalen diɣenna d imdewten belli d amaglay ɣer ṛuma
iḥulfa s ubaytel ikcem it u yesnezgem s tidet ad yanez ad ifek mayna yuzen ɣer uqensul sin imazanen ttuɣelfen ad ssutren tammazalt i netta kan d warraw is u ad yeǧǧ ayen nniḍen i wdakal n wegdud aṛumani maca at ikeffuten hastatus
iserdasen n udur amezwaru ssebdaden tufut tesɛa bla asurdu anaglam ur ssinen ara tugett n trebbuyaɛ
yella userdas aṛumani ima ara yessikil yettaẓay s teɛkemt yettawi yella yettawi lmuna n n wussan akk ifecka imrigan allalen n tɣuzi u yella yettnadi ɣef imeggawen iḥemmalen
wali s afellaasebter uṭun
mitilus ɣur s yagi tarmit uɣur tezwaren imenza s belli inumidiyen d at tiddas d wid yesmuttiyen adduden nsen
ɣef wayagi yemmuger imazanen yiwen yiwen u dduklen iḍall ɣef tulmisin nsen kra kra
s imi yeẓra belli mmutgen at qedcen yessenza ten s ureggen belli ad asen yefk yugurten d amuddur ma yezmer neɣ d lmegget
sakin iberreḥ d umyagar igerwen s tririt tamdagt ad t awin i wgellid kra n wussan kan zzeg s akin ikcem d ɣer numidya s yigen yettwasleɣmen akken yelha u yemmuteg ɣer imenɣi
ulac kra d isseflalayen di tmurt belli yella d inna imenɣi timezduɣin ččurent s madden actal d imakrazen deg wurtiyen d yigran
di temdinin d idewwaṛen teffɣen inabbaḍen igeldiyen aɣ d mmagren ttbegginen d amuteg nsen aɣ d fken irden d wallalen uɛebbi d kra n wayen nessuter deg sen ɣas akken mitilus ur yeǧǧi ara aḥezzeb am akken acengu ar d iteddu
yettaẓ ihi s yigen yemmuteg yettazen ifudas s uggug u di yal idisan illa ittɣill belli timatarin nni d wannuz d tikerkas kan
iswi nsent ad t sɣeḍlen deg wekmin ihi yewwi d tiḍaf netta s timmad is s trebbuyaɛ tifessasin d tufut n yiga yekkaten s yillan d wid yekkaten s yesmuden ma d tadfert yeǧǧa taggaẓt is i wmarag is kayus maryus s yemnayen ɣef yal iferr
yessedger inezzarfuyen iserdasen d inabaḍen n trebbuyaɛ imnayen imaragen s yiwet n yessemres awal n idewwaṛen i usuqel n wawal abuniqi d iskanenacluḥ agurbi iwakken ad yemyegmaḍ netta d temdint yettwafergen d igadiren
tarrayt d issekcamen inebbacen yid sen iwakken ad ceɣben tirebbuyaɛ n yemnayen ucengu ansi d uẓent
di tilawt yella yugurten yesɛa tamudi n tiddest d tmusni n taɣult d tarmit taserdasit d timeqqranin alammi nuɣal ur nezmir ara a nagad ma micki yella neɣ micki iba di tegnitt n imenɣi neɣ di tegnitt n tmazzalt
ur teggug ara ɣef webrid ideg yedda mitilus
yuɣ tella temdint tanumidit qqaren as baǧa tella d agdaz
yettaččar ugar di tgelda yakk anda yezdeɣ u yettaɣ u yeznuzu aṭas n iṭalyanen
aqunsul yesɛa iswi d asteqsi n imezdaɣ d uselmez diɣenna n ulemmas aserdasi ma yečča issers deg s tamastant iɛebba irden d isemmura n imenɣi
imi yalec yeqqar as d belli tugett n yemzenz yellan ad yessgellel deg imal asgalef n yigen u ad yageẓ ɣef wesgalef yellen yagi di tegnitt n tsekkirin agi yessekfeḍ yugurten anadi yettazen imazanen yettḥelli ɣef tmazzalt yettṛeggim itteqqen a d yessers yalec gar ifassen n mitilus slid tudert ines d tin n warraw is
aqensul iga ussis i wakken ad yesselɣed imazanen nni am imuzwura i wakken ad fken yugurten
zzeg s akin yerra ten s ixxamen nsen mebla ma ykfawel i ugellid s tifrat s tmazzalt yessutur
lawan nwemsawal yella yettgani asendu n ireggimen i as yettwafkan s ɣur imazanen
yugurten isemmenyaf imeslayen n mitilus d igiten ines u yegza belli ittnaɣ it s yemrigen is imi s wawal yettberriḥ d yebɣa tammazalt s tigawt yettnaɣ it s wuẓer
issukkes s zzeg s tamdint texxuter iḍall ɣef taɣult yettaram ad yesgufsu ineḍfaren ines taggara yestes imi t terra tmara ad yuɣal ɣer yemrigen u meskud aglam n taɣult yettak as asirem n trennawt yebda yettakez abrid yeṭṭafaṛ ucengu
yessegrew ayen iwumi yezmer n yigen u yesger iberdan wezzilen yerra d s tuffra igen n mitilus
deg wanur agi si numidya i yella isaḥ d ɛeẓrabeɛl deg beṭṭu yella ileḥḥu deg s wasif qqaṛen as lmatul yeffeɣ d seg wenẓul iggug s warem n igiman n uḍar s imisi syagi yeẓẓel yiwen umegganu n wedrar aquraṛ imsadayen d usaka n wasif agi ideg yeǧǧa wemdan war akraz
maca di tlemmast umagganu yagi
teẓẓel teɣzi n tmuɣli
yiwet n tewrirt yeden s uzemmur d ṛṛend d taggayin nniḍen n isekla tiwezzlanin igemmen deg wakal akiwal anijdi
ma d ayen yerzan taɣzuyt i d yezgan gar wasif d wedrar yella yeqquṛ deg wassar n waman
slid amur yudsen ɣer wasif wi ɣummen isekla iwezzlanen wuɣur ttruḥun imakrazen d wectal
ɣef tewrirt agi yeẓẓlen s wertak i wasif
am akken i d nenna yagi ires yugurten yak d terbaɛt is deg uddus yemmumi yella ireggem as i bumilkar s yilwan d kra iterrasen u illɣet as yebɣa ad t yeg netta yekcem deg wedrar s yemnayen ines d tufut n iterrasen
deffir mi yezzi i trebbuyaɛ d tkemmicin yettseggir itent u ittetter iten ad d mektin amezruy nsen bu yiseɣ d trennawin i d nḥella iḥellel iten ad mmestanen ɣef tmurt nsen d tgelda nsen mgal ajlaq tanaɣubt n ṛṛuman wagi i deg ara ddaw msenɣenizwar asenrnan t uzagluismutti anebbaḍmacaar ismutti iman
ka n wayen yessefken ɣef unebbaḍ ad t yeg iwakken ad yessenked imaɣlayen yelhan i yigen ines iga t ɣur sen yal igelman n taɣult ttwasleɣmen
acengu ur yesɛi ara iglamen agi
amdan nsen ur yelli ara d uddis ɣef win ucengu
ad ilin ihi mmutgen ad sɛun tanaḍt iwakken ad mguggin ɣef ṛṛuman imi ara sen yefk asillef
yusa d wass i deg ad zedmen akk ayen d sseḍṛan ntrennawin d wayen gan n wussis u ad t ssemnennin neɣ ad tili tectelt n tiṛẓi nsen yettaf awal ilaqen i yal aserdasamnaɣ ima ara t ikaz yefka yas kra n warraz w ad t id ismekti s tnafut agi u ad tid yesken d ahettu i wiyaḍ i lmend n tumast n yal yiwen ad iṛeggem ad yessummel ad iḥellel
s tewzel yessemres yal allalen iwakken ad ten issebɣes
tuɣ mitilus yetteder d seg wzdrar ɣef yixef n iɣallen is mebla ma yegza s tilin n ucengu s tuẓwayt yezra t
tazwara ur yegzi ara d acu tt tmeẓrut nni tajabalt i ywala maca inumidiyen llan ffren ger isekla tiwezlanin s yegmaren nsen macci d ayen isehlen ad ttwakazen
tulmast n temnaḍt yak d tissas nsen sdegen ten nitni d icenyalen isenǧaqen n sen maca ur iɛeṭṭel ara mitilus yuki i tqellaɛin u yenẓeḍ i yigen ines ad ibedd kra n wakkud iwakken ad yessetti udus n udeggi n imenɣi ɣef yiffer ayfus d yuẓen ugar ɣer ucengu issers iserdasen di kraḍ izarigen iwakken ad izmirent ad myellalent
issedger di tlemmast n tkemmicin wid yekkaten s yillan d wid yekkaten s ikuffa u yessers yak imnayen ɣef wafriwen
deffir mi d yefka kra n wawalen usebɣes i yewwten i waddad nni issader igen isɣer luḍa s nniḍam nni
maca imi yeẓṛa inumidiyen ur mbawlen ara ur iǧǧi ara awrir nsen rnu yeẓra nekẓen waman imi di n tsemhuyt unebdu illan yugad ad ten ineɣ fad dɣa yuzen amarag is mutilyus ɣer wasif ddant ɣer tama s kra n teɣlamin d timeẓyanin yak d kra n yemnayen iwakken ad yezwir yugurten u ad yefren adɣar i trusi n wegrur yella iɣill belli acengu ad inadi ad yessebded tikli n iṛumaniyen s waṭas n wenbac d ẓẓedmat ɣef iferrawen n yigen u ad bibilus mutilyus d amdakel n lilyus d skibyus d anezzarfu deg imeni mgal illa dagi d amarag n mitilus iǧǧ numidya s tdukli n uneggaru agi
yuɣal d aqensul aseggas dat sɛ
yettwarda zzeg s akin s tukerda tettwaɣtes turda ɣas ulamma adiwenni deg tbeddi yesmels it yennezli di smirn ad yesnuref iman is i tezrawt n usaḍuf rnu ɣer termit ines taserdasit illa d aggag d anmazray aneglam
yura timektiwin is yak d umezruy n ṛuma s tegrigit
war asurdu salustyus yeẓṛa ayen yura
yarem ad a ten ineɣ s fad d termuyt bla ma smarsen imrigen nsen zzegs akin mi yessudes iman is am akken teswaren imaɣlayen ibda yettaẓ s wudus nni wiyes d yuder yeǧǧa maryus deffir izarigen imezwura netta s yiman is yeqqim ɣer tama tazelmaḍt n yemnayen is i yellan zzat wemdadas
imi yeẓṛa yugurten belli tadfert n yigen n mitilus tezri izarigen ines imezwura yuzen akefful yesɛan lewhi n sin igiman iterrasen ṭṭfen iɣil nni wideg i d iris mitilus iwakken ad t yegdel ur itezzi ara ɣur s ma yeṛṛeẓyettwarna u ad yessemneɛ deg s
zzeg s akin ifka tamuli yeḍra d wemguggi ɣef ucengu zedmen inumidiyen ɣef yeffus ɣef zelmeḍ snegren tadfert nneɣ nneɣlen d deffir nneɣ utraren aɣ ssermin aɣ war anestem iserdan zzuzren yettwassnen s tebɣest d takdit yellan deg uddar amenzu zzat ucengu ḥaren baten si trenbaḍt nni i yḥazen akk igen tinnɣi
slid tuggsa iten d iḥazen seg wuggug u llan ur zmiren ara ad rren tiyitwin neɣ ad awḍen ɣer ucengu yugurten yella yessemter iderdasen ines yagi iwakken ad nnaɣen s uwexxeṛ ɣer deffir simi kan ara ten id yeɛnu ucengu s tdusi ur dduklen ara yak deg yiwen amḍiq neɣ tama s wakkenni ma ur zmiren ara inumidiyen ad ten qedlen deg weḍfaṛ n sen ad ɣellten tugett n iserdasen nsen iwakken ad ten ẓẓemlellin ad nnezwin u ad ten id wwten zzegs akin s deffir mi ten ssutlen
yuɣ lḥal tawrirt idurra ula deg tessuruf tarewla wala luḍa ladɣa igmar n yugurten nnumen aɛeddi ɣer isekla d ireccaten war ilɣiten ma d igmar nneɣ llan ttmagaren d tisiwaɣ n taɣult ur nnumen ara
rnu ɣer wayagi udem n tinnuɣi yella itetti ur yerkid ara d ucmit yesgeǧdir meskin userdas yennebḍa ɣer yemdukal is u ireggel seg ucengu wayeḍ yettwaḍfaṛ idarren bberwin illafen ttwaǧǧen zeddman ttarran mi ten id yemmuger wemha imrigen ikufa irgazen igemren imidawen icenga yalec yemmerwi ulac wara yesseɣden ulac wra ynebḍen asmma iman is yessudus yalec
ass diɣenna yuẓ ɣer uɣelluy tuɣult n tinnuɣi wer ɛad i d ban taggara imi tessafes tremmuyt d weẓɣal seg tedwast n yemnaɣen yesmaw mitilus d akken aẓdam n inumidiyen yufsas issegrew d irgazen is yules tuddsa n idurra ines u yemmuger s kuẓ n tgulaf tiṛumaniyin iterrasen n ucengu i yellan sɛan aṭas di tugett nsen ulin ɣer tewrirt ad sgunfun iɛenna iserdasen is iwakken ur ttaken ara mayna ur ttaken ara tarennawt i ucengu ara yregglan
nnig wayenni issumen asen d belli ur sɛin agrur wala asentel ara ten yuggẓen u belli imirigen nsen d nitni ken i d asirem nsen asuf deg wemnaɛ
yugurten si tama s ur di trebbuyaɛ neɣ tiyulaf yettwasuddsen seg iserdasen iṛumaniyen kan anemgal tgulaft neɣ tirebbuyaɛ yettwasuddsen seg inemyaqqanen
tagaluft tella tugda tis mraw n terbaɛt firqa
ibedd ɣer iserdasen ines ittseggir iten ixuz ara
imenɣi yettanbaḍ yessebɣas iten yezga yessegnay ineḍfaṛen ines i dissya ɣer da yettak asen afus n tallalt u tikkwal yessuddus ẓẓedma ɣef iserdasen nneɣ i yeẓra ɛyan u yettnaɣ d izerdak seg tuggugt
akka i myagaren sin inabbaḍen d imeqqranen dixataren myegdan deg wazal macci deg yeɣbaluten
mitilus yella yesɛa tabɣest n iserdasen ines annaren llan mgal is
ma d yugurten yalec yella ɣer tama s slid iman n yigen ines
taggara ufan belli tuɣalin ɣer deffir d awezɣi u belli acengu yugi imenɣi u belli iḍ la d iteddu
ṛṛuman nnesren ṛuḥen ad rsen akken d inna ussusel ɣef tewrirt agemmaḍ nsen
inumidiyen d ittwaẓɛen seg nnezwin u ṛṛzen cwiṭ yettwanɣa tugett tessaweḍ ad terwel s tnafut nurtured is yak d wenzaɣ nneɣ i yberdan di tegnitt wideg bumelkar iwumi iṛeggem yugurten s yilwan d kra n iterrasen am akken i d nenna s afella yuder d s yigen ines ɣer luḍa imi yeẓra rutilyus yezwar it di tegnitt i deg yella uneggaru agi yettazzal ad yezwir ɣer wasif anda yettusenḍa ad iṛuḥ bumilkar
ides di lɣerḍ is aɣawas i tinnuɣi mebla ma yettu tamagaẓt n yal amussu n ucengu simi yegẓa belli rutilyus yesbedd agrur is mebla asuedu imi yettali diɣenna wɛeggeḍ si tama wideg yettnaɣ yugurten
yugad ad inadi unarag ines ima ara yegzu s wayen yeḍṛan iwakken ara yegzem abrid i wmenzaɣ ines mi gwata yesseɣzef s n tinnɣi i yellan yagi yeddukel yessed ilmend n tedrest n tefles ines deg iserdasen ines dɣa wuddus agi i yes yeẓḍem ɣer wegrur n ṛutilyus
smawen iṛumaniyen s tuẓwayt isigna n aɣebbaṛ amedwas acku isekla imeẓyanen yellan ffren taɣult stullsen tamuɣli
ɣillen tazwara belli d aḍu i t id issekren maca smawen belli yezga deg yiwen weswir u yettaẓ ugar ilmend umussu n ucengu dɣa gzan s lemɣawla d acu i d taɣawsa uzzlen ihi ṛṛuman ɣer tuddma n yemrigen urren d awal i tsunḍa n tanaḍt gan idurra zzat n teqcelt sakin simi mlalen sin yegnan udem ɣer wudem neggzen wa ɣef wa s isuɣuten d unnigen
inumidiyen ur ṛeṣṣan ara tiririt ɣef yiman nsen akken i tt ṛeṣṣan ɣef yilwan simi ẓran iliwan nsen bberwin gar ifurkan n isekla tagnitt agi yemmerwin rewlen ǧǧan imrigen nsen s tugett nsen yessuref asen wudus n tewrirt d win n yiḍ ad ffɣen menɛen di talwit
jelqen asen kuẓ n ilwan u ttwanɣan yak yidaḍ yebbḍen kuẓet
taremmuyt n tikli leqdic di teqcelt tumert n trennawt
ayagi yak ur yegdil ara ṛṛuman ad ṛuḥen ad mmagren militus i agellel ines yesnuɣnuy lḥan d wuddus igerrzen ur ttun kra uḥezzeb acku tiqcelt inumidiyen ur tessuruf ara ideg i westehzi neɣ i wzaylal
simi d yeɣli yiḍ dderdiḥ n yezzi asen ucengu yfuṛsen i iḍaṛṛen n iserdasen ileḥḥun sɣillen igen isin belli d acengu la d iteddun ayen d isseglan aḥebbiṛ d herwel ɣur sin idisan tamsullest agi tella tezmer ad teglu s tunṭṭaft yesnuɣnuyen amer mačči d imnayen yettwaɣilfen ad mḍillen wa ɣef wa
imir nni s tuzwayt teɣli d tmendit deg yideg n tugdin
iserdasen ihi feṛḥen s trennawt nsen ttmesteqsayen amek i gan tamesseksalt nsen
yal yiwen yessumɣuṛ yesminig ayen yesker dɣa d tinna i tumast n tmeɣda di trennawt ula d imazdalen ɣur sen azref ad zuxxen imi di tiṛṛzi ula d izerluken ttḥulfun s ixḍan yezga mitilus deg teqcelt nni kuẓ n wussan iduwa imuggas s wartu yefka cciɛat tiserdasin i yebɣasen d yufraren u yesnemmer yesmineg yak tirebbuyaɛ isegger iten iwakken ad d smelsen tabɣest am tagi di tizziwin i yeggunin
u tid ur nelɣit ara imenɣi ilmend n trennawt ur d yeqqim ara di ssya d afella ad nennaɣ i wḥelli n igulaf di tegnit agi s dimmad is yuzen iserdasen i werwal d imazayen nniḍen iwakken ad d uɣalen s isalen ɣef yideg n yugurten s tiḍmi ines ma cwiṭ neɣ aṭas n iserdasen neɣ d igen yemmden i d as yeqqimen d wamek yessefrek tiṛṛẓi
yella ugellid yezzuɣer iman is yagi ɣer yiwet n tama d tiẓgi telɣet u tegder s ugama
d inna yessegrew tiduswin timaynutin yugar umḍan nset timezwura maca mebla amhaz wala arkad
tamnaḍt nni tettwahegga i tkerza n tyessawt ugar n wakken twuta i yimenɣi
d wagi i d agmuḍ yesḍullen i ywutan i ymensayen n inumidiyen ɣur sen ulac win yeṭṭafaren agellid yettwarnan
yeṛṛeẓ slid imnayen ines n tiḍaf yal yiwen yettṛuḥu anda yeffeɣ fell as annect a mačči d amalad ǧǧin
imi d tidak i d tiɣaṛiwin nsen
yegza mitilus belli agellid werɛad it s iburez ines ameqqṛan belli imenɣi ad iniyyer rnu ur ittekker ara alamma ira netta u abellen ur yettili ara yemsasa u belli acengu ad ibrar ad iṛṛeẓ u drus ara zlin iserdasen ines di trennawt ǧǧan imenɣi d tinnuɣin tuddisin
u yeɣtes ad isseqdec iɣaniben n imenɣi nniḍen
ikeččem di temnaḍin tinumidiyin tinesbuɣar ugar n tiyeḍnin
yessekreffet igamayen yettazeɣ yesseṛɣay aṭas n iɣeṛman d temdinin ur nesɛi ara igadiren neɣ ur nesɛi ara igadiren neɣ ur nesɛi ara timmastanin
ineqq imeggaden ubliɣen ur yettaǧǧ yalec i tḥeggast
seddaw unagraw n rrebrab am wagi ṭṭfen d ṛṛuman aṭas imekrafen akked timudiwin yeggten n yirden
d yal ayen ara yxedmen imenɣi yedra uṛeṣṣi asedsel n tmastanin di yal adɣar tent iswaren tisekkirin agi yak swawint d i ugellid tuggdin yugaren tiṛṛẓi yella iga asirem is yak di trewla
ma d tura yettwasdulli ad yezzuret acengu netta wer nessin amek ara yemmesten ɣef udaɣar ines
ad ittwazemlelli ad izdem ɣef idigan n ucengu
ɣas akken yeddem taɣtast i yeẓṛa d tufrint deg umaɣlay n wass a yeǧǧa tugett n iɣallen ines ad sgunfun di temnaḍt nni yezzuret mitilus ɣef yixef n tufut n yemnayen ines
itteddu deg yiḍ ɣef isakaten yettlen iwakken ur yettmeẓṛa ara
iẓḍem s tuẓwayt ɣef ṛṛuman yettwazmezren deg ugama
tugett deg sen llan mebla imrigen nɣan ten bbin aṭas inekrafen yiwen deg sen ur yemniɛ
zzeg s akin wexxren inumidiyen s weswar n tsunḍiwin ɣer taltin tinaragin zdat n waggad n kra n tallalin si tqcelt
di ṛuma tadawit tesmuta imi slan s trennawt n mitilus tunnigin amek i yesmares tuzulin n imenza u yeslal iten id deg iserdasen ines
amek i d issukes tarennawt s tugett n tebɣest ccil ur nelli ara yelha d wamek yuɣal d axaḍ di tmurt n madden amer i yeẓẓemlelli yugurten i yuɣalen d imzenger s tmentilt n wezdal n albinus
maca yuɣal ulac d acu ara t imenɛen ḥala tarewla neɣ antal deg ujulbi lqifaṛ i lmend useffugel s tedyanin agi tugrizin issusel useqqamu n yemɣaren ad sekren tizalliwin ad snemren iṛebbiten ṛuma tella alammi drus aya tettergigi ɣef yimal n imenɣi ass nni tedder tagnitt n tumert u yeẓṛa mitilus tamanegt akka i yessekfeḍ ussisen i wsenked n trennawt
d tizzalliwin timatitin anda ssenkaden iseflen d tmezliwin i yṛebbiyen tizaliwin agi sɛat asekkil n tmeɣra
yettekki yekk wegdud aṛumani d asnimmeḍ n iṛebbiyen ɣef trennawin i d ḥellan yegnen iṛumaniyen maca yezzubeẓ ad tesɛu asekkil n tuɣalin ɣer ṛebbi d wenɛar ɣur s yettaneḍ yes useqqamu n yemɣaṛen d ikehhanen ma d tanzeggit d abritur neɣ d aqensul i d yesgucculen azemz is u tettwasɣed i yall iṛebbiyen
ɣas akken iɛuss iman is iwakken ur yettak ara kra n tlemmiẓt i ucengu ur yettu ara belli tismin zgant ṭṭafarent taminegt s wudus skud yettḥulfu s timmuceɛt agar skud yettḥezzib ugar
yuɣal ur yessunuf ara i yiserdasen ines ad gen tasekkirt n waǧlaq
myebḍan deg wasmi sen iga yugurten akmin
imi ara hwiǧen tajjawt n yirden n uhicuṛ tuga imnayen akk ad agzen imɣuden
yella yettanbaḍ amur n yigen maryus yattnabaḍ amur wis sin
nnig wayagi yella yessekreffit tamurt s tmess ugar taḥeggaṣt
ssulin snat n tqeclin yal yiwen deg udɣar is maca ur yeggug ara yiwen ɣef wayeḍ
ttemsegrawen mi tesḍulli tegnitt
deg waddaden nniḍen llan ttmehhilen msebḍan iwakken ad d yeḍlen rrebrab
yella yugurten yeṭṭafaṛ iten teɣzi n tewririn yettnadi akkud d taɣult tameddizit iwakken ad yeg ẓẓeḍma s yella yessebluy aman tiliwa d tuga rrbiɛ di yal ideg ɣef yegza ad yekk ucengu
yettban d tikwal i maryus tikwal i mitilus iẓeddem ɣef tdeffert n yigen ileḥḥun u ad yuɣal ɣer wewrir iwakken ad yuɣal i tikelt nniḍen ɣer wagi ɣer winna
ur yettnaɣ ara maca ur aɣ yettaǧǧa ara iqudd it ad yesserked isenfaren
irwel unabbaḍ aṛumani deffir nneɣimi yeẓṛa iɣallen ines fessin s tiddas n ucengu i yugin imenɣi i yessutlen tamdint n tamdint ixxutren i yettusemḍen d alemmas ageldan amedru di temnaḍt
di teflest ines yugurten ad d yas s tdullit ad yefk afus n tallelt i yigad nni yettwasutlen
deg mi ad tili tinnuɣi
yugurten yella yelka s usenfar agi i kra n iserdasen imerwalen ihi yezwar mitilus s tikli izerben u yessawel i yimezdaɣ ad messtanen ɣef iɣulad nsen u ad ǧǧen ṛṛuman imerwalen yid sen i tallalt nsen
igad ur nezmir d awezɣi ad kerrsen i tikelt nniḍen
dɣa sselɣen amur imsenked ugar deg yigen ines nnig wayagi ireggem asen t s tasin ines di tegnit ilaqen
deffir tuṭṭfa n teɣtasin agi iṛuḥ ad yeffer deg iḍɣaren iɣelsen
ugar yesla s lemɣawla belli maryus yettwasuneḍad yennebḍu ɣef teɣlamt yides kra n tgalufin iwakken ad iṛuḥ ad yawi lmuna n yirden di tamdint tamezwarut i yeǧǧan deffir tiṛṛẓi s yuzel deg yiḍ akked tufut n yemnayen ines yeẓdem ɣef ṛṛuman tama n tewwura n temdint lawan i deg d ffɣen
imir imir iberreḥ i yimezdaɣ n sika iwakken ad ssutlen tigalufin nni si deffir dagi artum yefka yasen d talemmiẓt ttanaraft ma snen ad tt lemẓen
netta ad d yerr tagelda s nitni tilelli d taɣellist nsen
amer ur yezrib ara maryus s tikci n tanaḍt i tuggugt ɣef temdint s lemɣawla yellumzen tili ad t kersen yak imezdaɣ ma drus tuggett deg sen
ar tfesna agi i yellan ttmuttulen
iserdasen n yugurten ṭṭfen kra n wakud yessalet iten ttnegdamen inumidiyen tezzin ugellid nsen
maca imi yessekfeḍ ucengu aswar ines u xeṣṛen kra rewlen nnezwin
yewweḍ maryus ɣer zama tamdint agi igersen di tlemmast n usayes tella ur tettwafreg ara seg ugama
akken tettwafreg s umahil anaẓuṛ maca ur tt nkizen ara yeɣbayluyen tella d tanesbaɣurt s terbabt u s yergazen deffir mi yeddem mitilus tiɣtas timeddiziyin i teswar taɣult d imaɣlayen ibda yessutul tamdint s yigen ines yessamel i yal amrag ines alemmas n tenbaḍt ines
zzeg s akin tettunefk tmuli yeṭṭeṛḍeq uɛeggeḍ n imenɣi annect ilat si yal tamiwin mebla ma yessaged inumidiyen i yeẓṛan begsen u ɣetsen deg uɣyud igerrzen ibda imenɣi ṛṛuman yal yiwen yettnaɣ ad yizmir kra seg wuggug yekkat d s yillan n s yeẓra wiyeḍnin tteccḍen d seddaw igadiren
ama ad ten ɣeḍlen neɣ ad ten ṣken
ttnadin ɣef imenɣi yiwen
si tama n wid yettwasutlen llan ssegririben d iẓṛa ɣef wid i ten yessutlen i d yuẓn ugar neɣ ad d ḍeggren ikufa ula d kgudru yettekki i deg tefsi tkubrit tanga ineṭṭḍen i d ittak snuber merra teṛɣa ula d igad yegguggen ɣef igudar d imagaḍen ur asen yessuref ara imenɣi ttawḍen ten ikufa i yellan ttwaḍeggaren s ufus neɣ s icermaḍen u ssugsen aṭas deg sen amihi yessugda ten yak am yebɣasen am imazdalen ulamma iseɣ macci akken
skud yella imenɣi iteddu tuzzya n zama iẓdem yugurten s tuẓwayt ɣef teqcelt n ṛṛumanɣef uqeṛṛu n tdusiwin meqqrit
yeẓṛa yiwet di tewwura ur nettwadef ara akken iwuta acku llan inaḍafen ur ɣillen ara anḍaw am wagi s ɣur ucengu
nneẓwan xelɛen
uɣalen iserdasen nneɣ ttxemmimen kan amek ara menɛen iman nsen
yal yiwen s tarrayt ines kra s trewla kra s tuddma n terbabt aṭas i yettwanɣan i yettwaggṣen di yak amḍan
llan kuẓt n yergazen mmektan d belli d iṛumaniyen
dduklen sakin nezɣen iman nsen ɣer yiwen yiɣil i deg ur yezmir ara ucengu ad ten isnezwi ccil ussis iga ay gifen d akken ikufa i yes s i ten kkaten llan ttarran ten id ɣef ucengu s usmures ladɣa imi iɣallen ucengu llan ssden
micki uẓen inumidiyen llan sskanayen asen d tabɣes tameqqrant neqqen snezwiyen u ttarran ten zegglen
yella mitilus yettag ussis imi yesla deffir s dderdiḥ n ucengu immuqel ɣer deffir yegza bih bih belli imerwalen tmatart agi yelken belli d teddun d metwala is s ineḍfaren ines dɣa yuzen s imnayen ines meṛṛa ɣer teqcelt u s lemɣawla zzeg s akin maryus idd tigalufin n yemsasayen
lemɣawla ttwaɣendeg yebranen issuter it s imeṭṭawen s yisem n timmidwa i ten yeqqnen u s yisem n tegduda iwakken ur yettaǧǧa ara iseɣ n tigen i d iḥellan tarennawt ad yams u acengu ad iffertel war tamernut isselken maryus tanaḍt s lemɣawla
imir nni yeẓṛa yugurten amur n yergazen is ɣellin d si tqacuct n igecraraden wiyan iberdan ukmiren
iwakken ad d iffeɣ di twehhilt agini ideffer ɣef idasilen yettwaleɣten deffir mi yettwet
yeẓla aṭas n werǧaḥ
ma d ayen yerzan mitilus ideggr it uɣelluy n yiḍ ad ikcem s yigen ines ɣer teqcelt war ma isemmed taɣawsa s
deg wass nni d iteddun zdat ma yeffeɣ deg teqcelt i wsemmed n usutel
issegrew d mitilus zdat n teqcelt imnayen ines yak di tama i deg yezmer ad imager agellid yebḍa ɣef inezzurfa iserdasen tandaft n tewwura d iran n teqcelt
zzeg s akin iṛuḥ ɣer temdint ubberbez fell asen am yiḍelli di tegnitt i deg d iffeɣ yugurten seg unettul is s tuzwayt iberbez ɣef iserdasen nneɣ u yessker d rrebrab deg idurra imezwura kra n wakud maca uzen s lemɣawla fkan asen afus n tallalt
llan inumidiyen ur sɛin ara talemmiẓt ad zbun s teɣzi n wakud xas akken ssawḍen iterrasen nsen ad d swawin deg idarren nneɣ andal
ssallen iterrasen agi imnayen deg tamaskalt ad brebzen s akin ad wexxṛen am akken yella di tnamit n imenɣi n yemnayen maca nitni ttneyyiren aderrem ɣer zdat znezwayen tamterwit s userkes s tnaruft n tillit agi
imzaɣen d azgen i yterrasen nsen llan ttweddiɛen mmernan yagi
di tegnitt nnin s yiman is yella useqqi n imenɣi yeẓqel zdat zama
ussis yella yettusnemmes lumen ɣef tenqiḍin yellan ddaw tanaḍt n imaragen d inezzurfa iserdasen
yal yiwen ifulla ɣef yiman is ugar ma ifulla ɣef wiyaḍ
ssummen d imessutal anɣud s timmad is di yal idisan ttnadin ad mmeknen tiyitwin ugar n tririt nsent di yal adɣar asuɣu yemmerwin d usurers asuɣu n tdawit n umeǧǧed asqerweḥ n yemrigen yettali s igenni imsuden ṭṭaren si snat n tamiwin
yuɣ lḥal simi ara yessifes ucengu acemma ɣef imastanen n temdint ad d lhun s udafar anafag n imenɣi n yemnayen i yḍeṛṛun akin suggug snafalen d tadawit n anezgum nsen guncek ma yezzi imenɣi i wesmares n iwebrar n yugurten
llan ttberruḥen d sisemtiren ifassen ttanzaɣen ɣer zdat ttembawalen di yal tamiwin
am win yessinifen neɣ yettɛelli ikeffa
imi yeẓra ayen nni maryus yella d netta i d anabbaḍ di temnaḍt nni yessafes aberbez s tedmi isteɛmel iṛuḥ as usirem deg usmures
yeǧǧa inumidiyen smuzguten ɣer imenɣi n ugellid nsen s leɛqel
imi ten yeẓra ɣasen deg uḍfar s teɣdeft i ymenɣi iɣermanen nsen imir nni ineyyer aberbez s iserdasen is jgugulen agadir alammi usten ɣer tqacuct i yɣeṛman nsen s tekriḍt imir nni uzzlen d imettutlen kkaten ten id s yeẓṛa d times u s yal taggawin n ikufa
bdan iserdasen nneɣ s walluy maca kra n taskaliwin ṛṛẓent u ɣlin d igad yellan fell asent u rewlen wiyaḍ ayan iwumi zemren drus i ymenɛen
tugget ṛwan aggaṣ
taggara iga yiḍ tallest i ymenɣi gar snat tamiwin
yegza militus belli tirmiyin is yak i wkewwec n temdint ttwazerfent stuḍut
u belli yugurten ur yettnaɣ ara ḥala s tuẓwayt u deg taɣult tameddizit
u tella unebdu yekfa
inzeɣ iman is di zama u yessers timastanin di temdinin i as yunzen tigad iwumi yessuref waddad nsent agmawi d igadiren nsent ad mmestanent ayen d igran n yigen iṛuḥ ɣer tsefrest ines d yuzen di temnaḍt ɣer numidya
ma d netta bexlaf wiyaḍ ur yeslummeẓ ara asgunfu yagi deg uṭuṛṛes
imi imenɣi ur yettmehhir ara s terbabt iɣtes ad d yessenfel imenɣi s tiddas
inuda ihi ad yessali anguz imidawen mgal agellid ad yeslummez imekdiyen ines
immekti d dɣa deg wayagi bumilkar i d iṛuḥen ɣer ṛuma yeddukel d idd yugurten i yellan yerwel ɣef teɣtasin tanaḍin yettwaddmen mgal is ilmend n tmenɣiwt n misiwa ccil iseggiren ittwafkan argaz agi yella d amidaw n yugurten yugaren yak tikerkas n ɣef tedyanin agi wali taseddart d wayen tt id iḍefren di tilawt d yugurten i yefkan iseggiren agi macci d bumilkar u d netta i as inezḍen ad yeǧǧ ṛuma
yeslummez bumilkar imidawen nniḍen
yella ihi deg yiwen yideg ufrin yifen yal amdan nniḍen iwakken ad t yekneḍ iɛreḍ ad t yessenza s iṛeggimen iga yid s timliliyin tuffirin anda i as iṛggem s userhu ines belli ad d iḥelli seg useqqamu n yemɣaren mi yessaweḍ ad as ifek yugurten d amuddur neɣ d lmegget asuref yakk d tlelli n unizeḍ dag wayla s yunza unumidi s lemɣawla yella nnig tarmekdit ines tagmawit d yiwet tewtilt n urkawel di tegnitt n tifrat
tameddizit tamezwarut di ṛṛwaḥ ɣer umager n yugurten agellidn yella yennuɣni u yenniri ɣef uɣawas ines n yixiṭṭ yessemter it iḥellel it s imeṭṭawen ad isnezgem ɣef tallest ines d tin n warraw is d tin d wegdud i ɣef immestan di lebda neṛṛeẓ di yal imenɣiyen tekreffet tmurt nneɣ tugett n yergazen ttwaskerfen ttwanɣen tiɣbula n tgelda ttwakewwcent tabɣest n yergazen tettwarma akken yemmed ar tura yessefk ad d yaki izmer waddad azemmezger ines ad idegger inumidiyen ad mmagren taɣawsa d imeslayen am wigini yenẓa ugellid s wannuz
yuzen i unabaḍ aṛumani imazanen d iberrḥen belli yugurten yemmuteg iwakken ad yanez i yal imiẓiden u belli ad yessanez iman is i tmella n uqensul
imir imir yessawel mitilus i yigad yesɛan tafesna n yemɣaren seg iterrasen yellan ddaw tenbaḍin ines igad yesɛan tanzeggit iwakken ad yessileɣ aseqqamu nimenɣi
akka i d teqqar tanamit nimenza
s weswar n teɣtas n useqqamu agi yugurtern ɣer webri d n imazanen ines belli yessefk fell as ad ifek snat n twinas n igiman n iṛeṭlen lwezn is d lfeṭṭa d meṛṛa ilawen ines d tamuda n terbebt d yegmaren
imi yeḍra uselkem n tewtilin agi mebla agellel yettwanzeḍ s tikci n yal iserdasen imerwalen ad ttwaqqnen zzeg s akin ad tettwafek teggett deg sen akken d tenna teɣtast slid amḍan ameẓyan yellan yerwel ɣer muriṭanya ɣur agellid buxus
tazwara nni i deg bdant temsawalin n wannuz deffir mi as tettwakkes terbabt iserdasen is idrimen is
ssusnen yas s webrid unsib ad d yas s timmad is ɣer tizedyum iwakken ad yermes timadin n uqensul yesmutti turda ines i tikelt nniḍen deffir imi yeḥḥulfa yugel
u yugad tamernut n tidet ɣef uḍliben ines izma aṭas tikwal yettarra t ukasan ines i yir anyir
yessemyifi yalec ɣef imenɣi u tikwal nniḍen yessugun yeqqar acḥal yuɛer uɣelluy seg uǧaxfaf ɣer tmeɣda
taggara mi yefka d asfel acḥal n yeɣbula ɣlayen ineyyer imenɣi
imir nni di ṛuma yella useqqamu n yemɣaren mmeslayen msemtaren ɣef usedger n temnaḍin u yessesmel mitilus ɣer numidya
am wakken yebɣa usamma belli deg tegnit a dɣa anida yella kayus yesrusuy asfel timezla i yiṛebbiyen deg ɛutiqa yesla i yiwen n unekcaf yeɣra as d taseqqart is ay tizediyum quric lwad s wuggug n sa ɣef ugafa n usamer ɣef maǧaz lbab
wali gsell amezruy n tefriqt ugafa taqburt amḍan
asebter
d yeqqaren dakken yegguni t yimal d ameqran d axatar d ugriz yessefk ad yesɛu taflest deg yiṛebbiyen ayen akk yessugen deg tnellayt ines ad yessemres
yessefk ad yelken deg wayen yezmer ad t yermi
artum annect a ay as yehwan
yuɣ lḥal maryus yella ireɣ deg beɣɣu n uḥelli n tqenṣult u yella nnig wayen yesɛa yal tulmisin yessulfen i wakken ad tt id iḥelli slid tawacult tanaḍt taɣdemt tarmit ines yellan d tamanzalt taserdasit tuhriwt iman anaffag ɣer yimenɣi d amenzad deg temmazalt mačči d bu tugunt ccehwa d wedrim ur yesɛi ara tazitla slid tarennawt
ilul d yettwassegma deg aṛbinum anda ay yesɛedda akk temẓi is
simal yewweḍ awtay n urfad n terbabt ur yebɣi ara maryus ay yellan yettalek tazraqqa n yegrigiyen d zzhu n temdint
ur yebɣi ara slid tudert n teqcelt
din ay tella temrest turrizt
inefɛen ay igedlen iman nnes seg tebrer lefsad deg tegnit ay yessurfen ad yessemɣer deg s timecfiyin ines timekfiyin ines s lemɣawla
akken diɣ asmi ay d yemhez sdat wegdud ad yetter axawi n unezzarfu aserdasi ccil tuget n yiɣermanen ur t ẓrin werǧin addur ines i yiman is iqudd ad as yesger tuɣa n yal tiwsatin
seg yimir yezga yettali ixawiyen yiwen deffir wayeḍ yella yettag tizziwin ines deg yal taxawit s ɣas akken akk argaz a axatar s warur ines
deg tegnit a ma ulac acku tazitla ines ideqqer itt seg s akkin ur yebɣis ara ad inadi ɣef tqenṣult acku imir nni ma agdud yewweḍ ɣer yal tiwuriwin taqenṣult tella d tanureft d taglamt n yiheggaṛen ttemmeglin tt seg yiwen ɣer wayeḍ
argaz amaynu ay yebɣun yeg it d iweẓla i tegduda yella yettban d ur tt yuklal ara am wakken yumes s kra n yikiḍ
ihi maṛyus yufa dakken awal n yixid yettwaselkam gedged netta d tazitla ines
yessuter deg mitilus asgufsu akken ad iṛuḥ ad yessenked iman is
tuɣ mitilus ccil tabɣest ines d trennawin ines d waṭas n tlemsin tunnigin ines ur yettwassuref ara deg tzengert a talkawit imi d wa ay d amalad lɛib ay igerwen yal ilul d maṛyus aseggas n dat sɛ
yebda tamhelt n tserdast ddaw yiɣerban n ṛumans anda ay yella akked yugurten ddaw tenbaḍt n skibyu
gar twuriwin ay yesmares takusturit seg s akkin d agensas n tmata dat sɛ d afibritur
dat sɛ
seg s akkin d abritur deg sbanya taǧusant
neẓra dakken asaḍuf n likinyamus ay yettellin tiwwura n tqenṣult i tmeɣda lɛamma teḍra d tefrent fell as aseggas n
dat sɛ u belli lukyus sikistyus yella d aqenṣul amezwaru seg tmeɣda maca deffir twaɣilt n kana dat sɛ aydeg ibabb deg s uqenṣul n tmeɣda laṛkus traniyus faru taǧǧa n tmasit yesrus wegdud i tikkelt tis snat ɣef yiheggaṛen i usseddu n yimenɣi d trennawt tulkint sɣur wi ɣef hanibal aya yerra ten kewcen tawuri taxawit n tqenṣult nnig n tmidi lqern
iheggaṛen
deg tazwara yettwaẓwa s unadi a ur yegguni yiwen
u yessenfali d takunt ines atɛeǧǧeb i maṛyus u yessenfer it s uɣanib amidaw ur yessekcam ara iman is deg temsaksalt tawezɣit d ur yettmuqqul ara d asawen sennig waddad is mačči d azref n medden meṛṛa ad sɛun tazitla ɣer yal taɣawsa u ad yellez s wayen ay d iḥella
ur yessefk ara ad yessuter i wegdud aṛumani iseɣ
aserhu aydeg yesɛa azref ad as t yagi
imi ay llan yenciden a akk ttemyakken anzi ur tewlawel ara teɣtast n maṛyus
u tagara yuɣ as awal ad ideggi ɣef ussuter ines simi adamatu ad yessuref s wayen
asmi ay yettḥettit maṛyus seg s akkin ɣef ussuter is ifuk itt s wencad aydeg ay as yenna am wakken ay d nnan ur izerreb ara ad yili yewweḍ ɣer yewweḍ aɣ d wakud ay as yenna i wakken ad tnadid ɣef tqenṣul s uddukkel kečč d mmi
ladɣa aneggaru a yella yessemras tawalt taserdasit ddaw tenbaḍt n baba s
u slid lewhi n ɛecrin n yiseggasen deg wewtay ines imir nni tasegdelt a ur as terni i maṛyus slid beɣɣu n userhu d yiseɣ ay yessaram akked uksan mgal mitilus
yefka i tzitla d wurfan wi ay as yettakfen i isenfaren wi yuksan acḥal
yeslummeẓ tilemmiẓin akk akken ad yessemɣer leḥmala n ugdud i netta s tigawt neɣ s wawal
deg udeg n tsegrest yesban d amuzzu ugar n zik lmend n yiserdasen yellan ddaw tenbaḍt is
yettmeslay d yirgazen ikerwaten deg ɛutiqa ɣef yimenɣi s uɣanib deg s ajedder d tizzengert ddukklen ad ssersen ddaw uniẓed ines azgen n yiɣallen kan
kra n wussan kan ad qudden i tuqqna n yugurten amalway yesmezgir tagara n yimenɣi s tinnegmert
maca tikennaḍ ines d tizzengert ines tasnaraft iḥemmel nezzeh ad yenbeḍ azɣan a akk yettban d d tilawt imi teɣzi a n yimenɣi teswawi as d aṭad n tkemmawin
ma d ayen yerzan tallsa ulac ayen yetteddun s urured iqudden i lmend n wakken tebɣa
yella nnig wayen deg yigen nneɣ yiwen n unumidi qqaren as yuda mmi s n mestanabaɛl yerna d mmi s n mmi s n masensen yella mikibsa yessekles it deg ttewṣeyya ines d amekkasu seg tfesna tis snat
yekma t waḍḍan yessendudeɛ allaɣ is acemma
yella yessuter ad yers ukusi ines ɣer tama n uqenṣul am wakken tedda tnamit d yigelliden akked teɣlamt n yemnayen iṛumaniyen i tiḍaf ines yugi as mitilus la wa la winna iseɣ n ukersi acku ayen yerzan kan wid umi yuker wegdud aṛumani s wudem n yigelliden
ma d ayen yerzan imnayen ad yili d ixiḍ i yemnayen iṛumaniyen ad ttwamehlen d imḍafen deg tawalt n yinumidiyen
iṛuḥ maṛyus ad yemlil d yuda ay yellan ddaw taḍist n tuggut isegger it ɣef tiɣawt seg tlekkawt n mitilus ibeyyen as d tallalt ines u yesnafeg it s tmeslayt tukyist argaz a umi yessenḍuḍeɛ waḍḍan tigzi ines mačči tellid d agellid d tawgidt tameqrant s mmi s n mmi s n masensen ma yettwaḍḍef yugurten neɣ yettwanɣa i netta umi ara tuɣal tenbaḍt tagellidt
deg numidya imir imir u yezzubeẓ i uneḍru ad yefneɛ s lemɣawla
ma d maṛyus ay yettwaɣellfen s yimenɣi a s yisem is d aqenṣul
s tarrayt n yenguzen a yessenza yuda imnayen iṛumaniyen iserdasen ikelwaten kra ddan as deg lebɣi kra s ussirem ɣer tmazzalt htamen aceyyeɛ n tamawaẓt yimeddukal nsen deg ṛuma tibṛatin mgal mitilus d tarrayt ines deg usseddu n yimenɣi u ssuturen maṛyus ad yili d anebbaḍ
s wakka yettwassuddes umeqqun gar yinefranen ara d yerren lmendad u ad d ssalin maṛyus ɣer tqenṣult deg tegnit a s timmad is tella tmeɣda lɛamma tettmagar tihhugṛa yessemdudeɛ usaḍuf mamilya u tessuli irgazen imaynuten
s wakka yalec yuyen ad yessemres maṛyus
tebṛatin iṛumaniyen
inuda ad yesgufsu deffir mi yuɣal yugurten deg tikli n wannuz u yeɣtes ad ineyyer imenɣi yessiteb yalec s rrtu ameqran d lemɣawla yesserbeb igen yuses ad yerr timdinin ay t yeǧǧan s yiɣil neɣ s lbenna n tarrazt
yesselɣet idigen ines yessewken yuɣ d taserbabt tamaynut n ubeṛbez d tammastant d yal isemmura d yicermaḍen yessegdel fell as ussirem n tmazzalt
yessenzeɣ d ɣur s iserdasen n aklan tmaggaẓin nneɣ
s tewzel yewweḍ wermud ines ɣer yal taɣult u yessemres yalec
deg temdint n baga anda ay yewqem mitilus tamestant deg tazwara n yemsawalen n yugurten ɣef tifrat rran d awal yineflusen i unɛaṛ n ugellid i nnig wayen ur t ǧǧin ara s lebɣi nsen
gan anguz yid s ma d tamaɣda ladɣa ɣer yinumidiyen tella d mm tlumsut ay yettettin tḥemmel tamterwit d tilla
tessaram deg lebda asmaynet d tacengut n tifrat d usgunfu
deffir wemtawa sbedden slazekka deg yal friqeyya anda smidwinen u ttilint d tfugliwin timatutin aydeg ulac win ur nettekkay ara ass nni n tectut
ɛerḍen d akk medden inebbaḍen n twinest inezzurfa imserdasen anebbaḍ n temdint s timmad is turbilyus silanus nɣan ten meṛṛa lawan n tfugla slid turbilyus
sakkin berbzen yiserdasen yellan ttmerriḥen deg temdint mruzzaɣen war imrigen nsen am wakken yella waya d amagnu deg yimaɣlayen am wi
imi ban ɣaben inebbaḍen ɛudden ten lɣaci d tmeɣda kra gzan acku nnan asen yineflas s wanguz
ma wid ur yezgin acemma tumast nsen tenzeɣ ɣer waya imi ay ttafen lbenna nsen ay ten yettquddun deg tegnatit n trenbaḍt tamatut
ḥaren yiserdasen iṛumaniyen sdat umihi a ammeẓway ur ẓrin ara d acu ara gen dɣa nniẓden s usserkes taɣremt aydeg llan yillaf teqqel d alemmas i ucenga ay asen igedlen uduf
tiwwura llant ttwademmrent dat tkennaḍ gedlen ten ɣef trewla
rnu ɣef wayen tilawin d yigerdan ttemyezwaren ɣer uḍeyyer n yeẓra fell as sennig yizuɣen u s kra yellan gar yifassen nsen
am wakken yella d awezɣi fell asen ad sgedlen ɣef yiman nsen sdat umihi uslig am wakken yella d awezɣi ɣef win yugaren wiyaḍ deg tebɣest ad yebded yerṣa sdat tewsit tuhrimt
imulaɣ uṣliḥen imganaden imceṛṛiyen ibɣasen imazdalen ttwanɣan meṛṛa war tameẓla war asnuhyu war aẓubeẓ n ummesten deg tkesna am ta imi ay llan yinumidiyen s tebɣest mgal nneɣ u tamdint tdemmeṛ seg yal tama ala anebbaḍ turbilyus i yiman is gar wid ay irewlen seg yiṭelyanen ay imenɛen
is d tamella seg yimesnubeg ines i tiɣawt neɣ d agmuḍ n umsasa uffir neɣ d usamma kan ur neẓri ara
akken yebɣu yili argaz ara ifernen deg tegnit n wersan layas am ta tudert war aserhu ɣef wannag zeddigen yessefk ad yettwassemḍen d agacur d anebrur yennekma mitilus aṭas mi yesla s tedyant baǧa armi ay yeffer iman is ɣef medden
kra n wakud seg s akkin mmerwin wurfan d tekma u yefka taɣdeft akk ɣef usseklelli ay d yeḍran
iṛuḥ mi yeffel yiṭij yewwi yid s tarbaɛt yellan yid s deg tsegrest d tuget umi yezmer n yemnayen inumidiyen meṛṛa war imassen dduzan
azekka nni ɣef ssaɛa tis kraḍt yewweḍ ɣer yiwet n luḍa umi d zzint kra n tɣalltin timeẓyanin
din imi ay ugin yiserdasen is ad aẓen acku rmin ɛyan seg teɣzi n usurif yessusen asen assali ay d yennan dakken tamdint n baǧa ur tgug ara ugar n wagim ma aṭas yenna asen yessefk fell awen ad tesferkem tarmuyt war asmummi u ad temmutgem ad terrem tiɣawt ttaṛ ɣef yiɣermanen nwen yugaren deg tebɣest d ugacur
ccqa
deg tgara berqent deg wallen nsent tbaɣurin n yiglafen
s wakka ay d yessker ay d yessemsed tabɣest nsen yenzeḍ imnayen ad nnezwin deg tezwert iterrasen ad aẓen deg yidarren yemlalen anect umi zemren u ad ffren illafen nsen
imi ay ẓran yimezdaɣen n baǧa igen yettaẓ ɣer sen ɣilen deg tazwara dakken d mitilus dɣa akken ay yella lḥal uzzlen medlen tiwwura maca s lemɣawla unan belli urtiyen ur ttwaskerfen ara u dakken iserdasen ay yellan ɣer sdat d imnayen inumidiyen ssugnen s wegmaḍ dakken d yugurten u mehzen d ad t mmagren s unafag n tdawit lfeṛḥ tameqrant
s tuẓwayt neṭwen yemnayen d yiterrasen ɣef tikkelt kra nɣan lɣaci yellan uffuɣ n temdint kra uzzlen ɣer tewwura kra ḥewṣen lebṛuj urfan d weqlal ḍḍmeɛ n uḥelli n weglaf llan rnan taremmuyt
akka sin n wussan kan ay sɛan gar yifassen nsen akken ad ssetbennen tikerras n yinabbazen
tamdint a tameqrant tanesbaɣurt tettwafka tamudi n sin n wussan i tḥewwaṣt d tiɣawt
anebbaḍ n temdint turbilyus ayɣef d nemmeslay sufella d netta kan gar yiserdasen is ay izelɣen imenɛen
yessawel as mitilus ad d yaf tafakult ayyes ara yemmesten ɣef yiman is imi ay yebrar yerna yettwarda yettwet s teɣri yettwakkes ugerruj is imi d aɣerman alatini
deg tegnit a s timmad is bumilkaṛ ay yellan yessugen takti n wannuz i yugurten maca yuɣal yeǧǧa tt yella uẓubaẓ i rutilyus ad yezleɣ ad yemneɛ seg tmernut s tilin ines d aɣerman s yinz n usaḍuf lifya n useggas dat sɛ
aya d talemmiẓt i maṛyus ad yesseɣrebbet mgal tameẓla n mutilus i usaḍuf
wali acku yugad yuɣal teḍfer it turda ɣer ugellid ay yeqqlen yetturduy
yessarem ad yeffeɣ seg waddad a yerna yesnezgem s telqey deg yiḍ deg wass yettnadi tiddest ara as yessurfen ad yessertek asaḍ ines tagara imi ay yessemres akk allalen ay izemren ad ten id yessugen yessemres ad d yaf ayetliṭ d yiwen seg yineflusen d aheggaṛ d anesbaɣur yesɛan annaz ɣer yiɣermanen ines
d netta deg tnamit ay yettnabaḍen igen micki ay iba ugellid u fell as ay yella
yettfullu i wseḍṛu n yal iwuẓla itaremmuyt ur as tessuruf ara ad ten yesker ɣef iwuẓla i as yettaǧǧa micki llan wid yexxutren ugar i yet yeggunin
taflest nni yesɛa deg s teswa ɣur s iseɣ d tirruffeht
msasanihi di sin yid sen u sbedden as taxazabitayen nniḍen ǧǧan t ad as xemmen di lawan is akkan i teswar tegnitt
iṛuḥ nibdalsa ad yernu ɣer yigen uɣur yettwanẓeḍad t yeǧǧ ur yeggugi ara ɣef tsegrest n ṛṛuman iwakken ad ten yegdel ur ssekreffaten ara tiferkiwin war tamarnut maca yergagi deg uḍlib yettwaɣewsen
ur d yusi ara di tectut ittwasbedden tugdin is wexxrent asemres n tɣawsa
akkenni bulumkar iḍemɛen deg uselkem n usenfar i yugaden diɣenna ad iwexxer imezdi ines ɣef uɣawas nsen u ad t yessenfel s uɣawas nniḍen yuzen as tabratt ɣef ufus n yergazen i asenfar nniḍen ur yezmir ara ad yili ḥala akaz aqirri i yugugrten s txazabit i yettwasuddsen mgal is maca bumilkar di tugdin ines yessemyif ur yettsemmi ara tiɣawsiwin s yismawen n sent am akken d inna salustyus
yetteflas deg sen
yessugnut it deg s ɣef uzmay is d wezdal is deffir mi yeggul s iṛebbiyen imaɣlalen is yebɣa tura ad yeti uṛeggem n mitilus d akreffu fell asen yugurten ifuk ay d yegran slid anegzu ma ad at tneɣ tebɣest is n tin n mitilus iwakken ad yefren d acu yessemyif tarrazt neɣ tamernut
iḍṛa wemtawa belli imi tettwaṭṭef tebratt agi yella nebdalsa yuɣal d seg ulaɣmu n waddal yermi u yeẓẓel ɣef umetṛeḥ ines deffir mi yezga s tebratt n bumilkar iḥulfa s taẓeyt n unuɣjef
ifka mayna i yiḍes am akken tḍeṛṛu di tnamit mara yebberwi wallaɣ
yella yesɛa yiwen unumidi yesɛa deg s taflest d leḥmalayesselḥuy tadbelt n iweẓla ines
yessenyakk isenfaren ines slid aneggaru agi
imi yezga s waggaḍ n tebṛatt yedma belli aṣaḍ ines yeḥwaǧ it am umagnu ikcem ɣer wecluḥ n nebdalsa iṭṭef tabratt nni yeǧǧa uneggaru agi ɣef tsumta war arrtu u netta yeṭṭesiɣra tt id di tazwara ɣer taggara
izga s wakka s txazabit yuzzel ɣer ugellid
yuki d nebdalsa zzeg s akin s cituḥ ismaw dakken tabratt nni ulac ittyegza d acu yeḍṛanyurem di tazwara ad yakez mbawa i d acekkam imi ur yegzi ara yuzzel ula d netta ɣur ugellid yessarem ad a t yesserked yenna yas yenna yas belli takerrast n uxeddam is tḥeggef it degg ayen yebɣa ad a t yesker s yiman is
di tegnitt nni s yiman is iḥellel it s imeṭṭawen s yisem n tmidwa i as d ibeggn di lebda u mazal timaterin n tekdit ṣeḥḥant ar yimir
iḥellel it ur yessugun ara belli yezmer ad as ig aḍlib am wagini
iffer ugellid iḥulfan is idettiyenu yerra d s laɛqel
tqudd tmenɣiwt n bumilkar d waṭas yigad yettekkin di txazabit yeffer urfan is yugad ad yeswawi tanekra ma yesduqqet tamernut maca deg yimir war yessin yugurten tafrawt la deg wass wala deg yiḍ
yal adeg yal amdan yal akud ɣur s yettwarda yattagad kif kif ineḍfaṛen d icenga ines tiṭ ines d taɛessast
yal aɛeggeḍ yessexlaɛ it yessenfal yal iḍ i yiḍes war ma yga azal i waddur ines tikwal yettaki d yexleɛ yettazzal ɣer yemrigen ines u yessawal i tnekra
yella itedder di rrebreb yuzen ɣer yisiḍ
yesla mitilus nnan as iserdasen imrewal s wayen yeḍṛan i bulemkaṛ d usekfel n tyxazabit dɣa ineyyer s lemɣawla asiteb am akken taluft terza imenɣi amaynut
maryus yesḍuqqet aḥettet ad iṛuḥ ad yesgunfu imi yeẓṛa ur yenfiɛ ara ma yeǧǧa t nnig lebɣi s ladɣa imi d win yuksan idegga yas ɣef tesgunfutt ines
ɣef wakken d inna blutarxusur yessireg ara mitilus i maryus i wakken ad iṛuḥala mraw d sin n wussan zdat tefranins usirem ad yaweḍ yugel maca maryus yessaweḍ ad yegzem asurif seg teqcelt ɣer usagen n ɛutiqa di sin wussan d yiḍ
yagi imir nni d tamzizla izaden ma d azgar n yillel ur yezri ara nnig kraḍ n wussan
di ṛuma llan meddan fuǧǧen ɣef tebṛatin yerzan mitilus d maryus u mmugren s tdawit ayen d nnan ɣef wagi d winna
tihhugra n unabbaḍ ur tuɣal ara d azwel n userhu tuɣal d azwel n unezgum
tanefrat n maryus ur as d rni ḥala taɣerfantrnu ɣer wayenn i tinadin itezzin ɣef wayagi neɣ wayenni d yeswawin yiman anakbar ugar n wayen d swawin iruren d imaladen n yal yiwen deg senrnu ɣer wayenni inebbaḍen imzermanen i gezgan smerkayen d lɣaci u ssuturen di yal agraw s uqerruy n mitilus u smeɣren iruren n maryus
u taggara nsen smerkayen d lɣaci alammi inaḍen ikerrazen ǧǧan amahil nsen awfusan igellan d abaɣuṛ d taɣbalut tansuft n sen
ǧǧan amahil iwakken ad ddun d maryus flan tiweḍwafin n sen tugmudin ad ssegren asmures ines
ayagi yak zdat iheggaren
tuɣal tqensult ɣer wergaz tiddehcert n ameynut
deffur iseggasen ɣezzifen n tɣerṣi zzeg s akin agensas n tmeɣda tibiryus manlyus mankinus tsemter tameɣda ɣef win iwumi yettwafek useddu n imenɣi mgal yugurten
irra d wegdud s yiwet n taɣect i maryus u yuɣal s wayenn i d taɣtest yeswetlen lammi aseqqamu n yemɣaren zdat yimir nni s kra kan n wakud isseɣlef mitilus ɣef numidya war asemdu
deg wammas n wayenn i yugurten ɣlin as yemdukenal is
kra mmuten ɣef ufus is tdegger iten tugdin ad rewlen ɣer ṛṛuman neɣ ɣer ugellid buxus u yegza belli askar n imenɣi yettaser imamilen u yeẓṛa d akken d amihi ad ifulla wemdan ɣef tneflast isekkiwen imaynuten deffir mi t kenḍen yeqbuṛen macci yiwet n tikelt
yettban d yezma u yennuɣref yezga yesmummi
yalec yettban as d d anessarfuf irgazen tidyanin isenfaren
yal ass ad yesmetti taɣda
kif kif imaragen
tikwal ad ibberbez icenga tikwal nniḍen ad yekcem di tlemmast n tneẓruft
d amagnu ad yessers asirem is deg trewla cciṭuḥ kan
zzeg s akin deg imenɣi ur yeẓṛi ara ma ad yeǧǧ taflest ines di tebɣest is d tekdit ineḍfaren is
neɣ ad iḥezzb ad iḥareb anda yemmuqel slid icenga i gẓeṛṛ
di tlemmast n teglalit agi
iban d mitilus s yigen ines
yennezwa yugurten i yellan ur yesɛi ara akud iqudden wakken ad yesserbeb igen is w ad t issudes
ibda imenɣi dinn a anda yella ugellid zban inumidiyen kra n wakud u ṛṛzen anda nniḍen simi teḍa temlilit tamezwarut
kecmen iṛumaniyen tamakta n yemrigen d illafen maca ciṭuḥ kan inekrafen acku di tnamit inumidiyen d arured nsen i ten izellɣen deg imenɣi ugar n yemrigen nsen
iserdasen imerwalen d umur n yemnayen ines
yebbeḍ ɣer tala d tamdint tammeqqrant u d tamesbaɣuṛt anda llant tesbaynutin d yeɣṛem anafrac i deg llan warraw is
imi yegza s wayenn i mitilus ur yezmi ara wareg ccil is yegza nezzeh belli ger tala d wasif d yuẓen teẓẓel tmurt s teɣzi n smuset mills maca asirem n uḥelli n temdint yefka yas aseddiren n trennawt n yal iswaɣen d unaẓar n ugama s yiman is
ɣef way agi u s uniẓed zzeg s akin ssersen d aggaten yak ɣef iɣeṛṣiwen uɛebbi
slid aggaten n yirden ara yqudden i mraw n wussan d yeqṛaben d yal ijeqḍuṛen yettawin aman
rnu ɣer wayagi issegrew d s ɣur imezdaɣ n ugama ayen iwumi yezmer n iɣersiwen i ɣef iɛebba ijeqḍuṛen n yal taggaytladɣa ijeqḍuren n wesɣaṛ i d yewwi deg igerbiyen n inumidiyen
nnig wayenni issenza imezdaɣen n temnaḍin d izzin igad i as yunzen deffir trewla ugellid iwakken ad as d awin ayen iwumi zemren n waman
issebded asen ass d wedɣar n tihawt
yuɣ d diɣenna ɣer wasif agi i ɣef d nemmeslay s afella
tineqqiṭ taneggarut dat temdint ibbi iɣyal ines n uɛebbi n waman inil ɣer tala
imi yewweḍ ɣer wedɣar i yesbedd i yinumidiyen
simi yessuli tiqcelt ines d ufrag is nnan d yewet d ugeffur s waṭas alammi iqudd ugar assaren n yigen
rnu ɣer wayenni tamakta n waman d fkan inumidiyen tekka ɣef wayen ɣillen acku imdanen agi am akken tḍeṛṛu d yegduden yunzen drus aya ḥeṛṛṣen iwakken ad rnun ɣef yekfawalen nsen maca iserdasen s uḥulfu nsen ajjadan fernen aman n ugeffur
tadyant agi tettekki deg usali n unafag nsen nẓan belli iṛebbiten imaɣlalen ttɛeẓẓiṛen s teɣḍaweft tunegmiḍt fell asen
azekka nni s wemyazal i wayen iɣill yugurten wwḍen yegnan nneɣ ɣer tala
ddhecren imezdaɣ i yɣillen belli ttwasmetnen s yilɣiten n tmennaḍt
ulamma tabɣest n iserdasen nneɣ tesdehcer iten maca ayagi ur ten yegdil ara ɣef usmuteg i ymenɣi u d ayen igan iserdasen nneɣ
maca agellid yeẓṛa belli ulac i yellan d awezɣi tura s afella ɣer mitilus
is ur yesmaneg ara s yigen ines yal illɣiten imrigen n weẓḍam neɣ n imestan taɣult tasemhuyt taggara agama s timmad is u d netta i d aṣaḍ imineg irwel ugellid di temdint deg yiḍ
ddan warraw is d umur ameqqṛan n ubaɣuṛ is deg wass nni yuɣal ur yettɣimi ara nnig yibbas neɣ yiḍ deg yiwen wedrar
s tfakult belli iweẓla ines swaren zzerb agi di tilawt yella yettaǧa d tikerras u yettarem ad sa yessinef s lemɣawla n umussu iɣill belli aselkem n tidmawin am tidak nni teswar akud aɣezzfan imaɣlayen imeddiziyen
iẓṛa mitilus si tama s belli imezdaɣ ɣetsen ad mmestanen u belli tamdint tella tettwasten s tudsa ines s yideg ines irna yezzi yas d weḥfir nnig s afrag s ibudiden uɣanim d ifurkan d wakal yelha ad sbedden i ticket lebruj tabrar
tamsalt nsen fell as iwakken ad yemmesten ɣef usuk d inemmuhal si tama nsen igad nni yettwasulten slallen allalen nsen n taggazt
s tewzel yiwen ur yessewzeg
i snat n tamiwin di kra
taɣawsa agi teswar kuzet n wussan n wussis ukmir si tama n ṛṛuman rnu imenɣiyen ukmiren ad d ḥellin tamdint kan ma d igelfan ssekrefften ten iserdasen i yrewlen imi ẓṛan iɣṛaben ɣellin s tyita n taneggarut yilliten u ssekrefften akk ayen d sgerwen ɣer teɣṛemt tageldant awreɣ lfeṭṭa d wayen yak yesɛan azal ɣer yemdanen ay agi deffir mi swan lammi sekṛen
u fkan times i wfaɣur nni yak d taɣṛemt d yiman nsen
s wakka nebḍen ɣef yiman nsen s wangaẓ angaẓ i sɛan azref ad t qaden s ɣur imerniyen
imi nebzen ḥellan tala usan d si temdint n lebda igensasen ssuturen din mitilus s uḥellel ad asen yazen tamestant d unebbaḍ yella hamilkaṛ qqaren d d argaz aheggar u yettwassen s tiddas ines yettnadi ad isiɣ times n tilla di temdint
la tenbaḍt n inabbaḍen wala tanbaḍt n isuḍaf sɛan fell as tazrart influence
ma ur d issekcem ara iman is mitilus s lemɣawla ad d afen iman nsen u nitni d imyaqqanen d ṛṛuman zdat imahiyen d imeqqranen
neẓṛa ɣef webrid n abyanus angaz i yes yenbeḍ mitilus ɣef iserdasen irewlen yegzem ifassen i kra
yenḍel kra alammi d talemmast n tidd iwakken ad ttwasekren d nnican i yserdasen ines u ad ten yessreɣ d imudduren ar tagara
di tilawt llan imezdaɣ n lebda deg mi yebda imenɣi ssuɣden mgal yugurten ṛuḥen ɣer uqensul bistya zzeg s akin ɣer ṛuma tettren tamidawit d tamyeqqna yid neɣ u deg wasmi tt id ḥellan zgan d imsasayen nneɣ imekdiyen ttaznen i yiziḍen n bistya d albinus d mitilus s lemɣawla ɣef waya i asen yerra s wendag yuzen asenkuẓ n tgalufin
liqunya kayus albinus d inabbaḍen
d iṣuriyen i yessentan tamdint n lebda iga ɣef d nnan belli d imennuɣen di temdint i d tamentilt n tuffra seg tmurt nsen
usan d ɣef webrid n yillel u udren d di tama yagi tezga d ɣer snat
sirta iwumi yuɣal usemmi nsent ɣer tulmist n iftasen agi s timmad nsen
di tilawt yella d ifriqya sin yeslulla
s tehri ur nemsegda maca yiwet n tumast nsen s wudus talqayt tameqqrant s wudus ɣer weftas di yal idigen nniḍen s tigin n usamma d ileblaben kra asserḍaben t kra ssɣaren t acku simi ara yenhewwal yillel ad d izuff ttdeggirent d timdeswal lmujat yalec yid sent aluḍ ijdi ula d iftusen n teẓra akka d aḍu i yettagen tazrirt u yessetti udem n tilawt ula d isem n sirt yettwasuddem d deg umyag nzeɣ tirer tutlayt n imezdaɣ n lebda iman is temmutti qqaren tettwassen aseggas dat sɛ
uggug usamer anamek is ger tunes d tmurt n ṭṛables
si tama nniḍen deg tegzi n yeqbuṛen tettusemḍen maṣer d abruy si asya
ninenti d sirt ameqqṛa asallu n sirt di libya d amezyan
asallu n gabes di tunes
tidyanin n s usemdu n userwi idd inumidiyen u jebṛen tugett iṣaḍufen d imsayen n at ṣṣuṛ ayagi ladɣa d ayen i lemden fell asen imi teddren ggugan ɣef udabu alemmas gar asen d umur yeččuṛen n numidya ẓẓlent ṣṣḥaṛi d tallunin imi lebda ssawḍent aɣ d ɣer temnaḍin agi iban iyi d iwuta ad d smektiɣ timeggit talɣuɣant tugrizt n sin iqeṛtaǧiyen i deg sen yesmakta yi d yidegdi lawan wideg tella qeṛtaǧa d taṣaḍt n umur ameqqṛan di friqya tella yas am tmenzaɣt qurina tanesbaɣurt
taḥernukt teẓẓel gar snat n temdinin agi yiwet n temnaḍt d tanejdit ttagellant ulac la adrar wala asif ara yettwasmersen i uṛeṣṣi n tilas nsent ayen dɣa d iswawin aṭas n imenɣiyen d idammen gar snat n tmura agi
si snat n tamiwin d ignen d tunawin ddgedgen ṛṛẓen i sin yegduden sfuken tiduswin nsen
ugaden am win yernan am win yettwarnan ad uɣalen d taɣtast n yimzerner amaynut mtawan diɣ netta ɣef temmazalt u ad azzlen sin yemzazzalen seg snat n temdinin
deg wass ara yettwasbedden u ad yili wedɣar i deg ara mlilen d netta i d tilisa gar asent sin yeɣlalen
tuzen qeṛtaǧa sin watmaten filinus i yeg gezmen abrid s lemɣawla d tameqqrant
iquṛniyen lḥan s leɛqel
is ayenn i yekka d di twenkaẓ n tmezwarut si tama nsen neɣ d tmiḍrant i d yusan s usamma ur ẓṛiɣ ara di temnaḍin agi
am akken iḍeṛṛu di tlemmast n yillel aṭas n ssemyifen ten yegrigiyen nni tikwal i deg aɣ yesbedday uleblab ɣef taẓin ɣer zdat imi ara d yezzef waḍu ɣef ifettiḥen n luḍa ur nesɛi ara n tuga yesskaray d ijdiyen ijdiyen agi ttwadeggaren deg tjenfeḍt d tazwart yettaččar yimi d wallen n imessikel u ad t yesswaɣ ɣef tmeẓṛiwt zdat s u ad t yessegri ɣef tikli
akken yebɣu yili imi samawin sin iquriniyen nni belli nneǧran u ugaden tamernut i ten yeggunin imi ara uɣalen ilmend n ugellel agi amihaw ɣef teɣḍewfft n tmurt nsen
ttwardan sin iqertaǧiyen nni belli gguren zdat wakud yettwasbedden ugin ad slen i kra yalec llan ẓeṛṛen t yif tuɣalin yeṛṛẓen
ssutren iqertaǧiyen asebded n tewtilin timaynutin maca ad ilint d timegda imir nni ad ttwaneḍlen d imudduren deg yideg i ssuturen d tlilist i tmurt nsen neɣ ad ten ǧǧen ad aẓen s tewtilin nni s timmad nsent annect bɣun
yedra uheggi ɣef wemtawa
fkan sin ifilaniyen nni iman nsen d asfel ɣef tmurt nsen diɣ netta neḍlen ten d imudduren ṣkan asen iqeṛtaǧiyen tafacka deg igen nni s timmad is
tifackiwin yewwin ismawen nsen sersen asen timayin nniḍen di qertaǧa
ad d uɣaleɣ tura ɣer usentel inu
yega yugurten deg wasmi as tṛuḥ tala belli ulac kra n tdusi i yzemren ad tebded zdat mitilus iṛuḥ did kra n yergazen ɣer ugens n tneẓruft iweɛren alammi yewweḍ ɣer lǧitul d agdud amezzawru d amaziɣ i yellan alammi d imir nni ur yessin ara isem n ṛṛuman
tagensast ɣer ṛuma yessutur issegrew d iɣaci agi ciṭuḥ ciṭuḥ yesnam asen asuddes deg idurra d tikli deffir n yillaf d uselkem d tinbaḍin
s tewzel akk ayen yerzan iwezla iserdasen
rnu ɣer wayagi yerna d ɣer udar is igad yuzen ɣer ugellid buxus s isefkiyen imeqqranen d uṛeggem s tallalt nsen
yurem asqenzeɣ n ugellid agi s tḍullit n ukeččum ɣer imenɣi mgal ṛṛuman
uyessemres deg wayenni s tlemḍi tameqqrant acku buxus yella yuzen di tectelt n imenɣi agi timmidwa nneɣ
asummer agi ines yettwamager s tuggut ulamma yurrez aɣ deg imenɣi agi
yeḍra wayagi deffir tiddas n kra n yergazen i yesderɣel uqulal temɣer uɛebbuḍ i gennumen tamjajjawt s wayen yettarzen d wayen ikemmun rnu ɣer wayagi yella yugurten ɣur yiwet di yessi s n buxus maca di tillawt tamaqqant agi ur telli ara ɣur inumidiyen wala ɣur imuriṭaniyen d tamaqant yudsen
yal yiwen yettaɣ di tlawin ayen i as yessuref ubaɣuṛ ines kra ttaɣen mraw kra ugar ladɣa igelliden
s wakka i tettṛuḥu leḥmala di tuggett agi ula d yiwet ur tettaṭṭaf adeg n tnaragt tadattit ur tesɛiḍ i gettḥulfu ɣur sent
myegrawen sin yignen ihi deg wedɣar iɣef mtawan sin igelliden deffir mi msenfalen tamequnt
iga yugurten inaw i deg d ismerk adeggal is mgal ṛṛuman ṛṛuman d imdanen imekraḍen imzenanen d at uqelal ṭṭmeɛ d nitni i d acengu imezdi n tmaṭṭi ɣur sen yiwet n tmentilt n imenɣi mgal buxus mgal n yugurten d mgal n waṭas n yegduden nniḍen
ayagi tamentilt is d fad fuden ɣer weɣmard wenbaḍ zzerren acengu di yal tadusi yellan mačči d tadusi nsen
assa yugurten iḍelli qeṛtaǧa d ugellid azekka
yal agdud i yebɣu yili t d acengu n ṛṛuman
ma iban d d udmis deg wallen nsen
deffir umeslay agi d wiyaḍ rewsen ɣer wigini
ɣetsen sin igelliden agi ad nebzen qiṛta anda yella mitilus isguder iglalen d inekrafen d imassen di tedmi n yugurten ama ad yenbez tamdint iman is
u ad asen yefk irez n wussus nsen di sin
ma iruḥ d unebbaḍ aṛumani as d ifek tallalt ad sɛun talemmizt ad mcubbaken yid s acku ɣur unumidi bu txidas ulac taɣawsa izerben am usewḥel n buxus deg umyegdal ɛinani d ṛṛuman
imi yugad ad yefren buxus acku aṭas i yegguni ayen nniḍen wala imenɣi
idra wemyaqqan ger yugurten d buxus aseggas dat sɛ
aseɣli n qerṭaǧa iḍra dat sɛ
tiṛẓi n birsi agellid n meqdunya deg imenɣi n bidna aseggas dat sɛ
qirta d qessentina n wassa tamaneɣt n numidya imir nni wali taseddart ad d nesseglu deg wesɣal agi belli tamdint ikewwec itt mitilus lawan n temḍugt is deg unebdu n useggas maca salustyus ur yesɣil ara di kra n yideg ɣer tallit agi n imenɣi
macci am akken yennum ittag deffir tiṛṛẓa n yugurten di yal taɣult i yebɣun tili tt
iṛeṣṣa akken iwata adasil ines ur yeggugi ara ɣef qiṛta
d inna yegguni ten iɣil yif it ad yissin imuriṭaniyen imi aweẓlu n wass nni yerza icenga imaynuten iwakken deg yimal ad yizmir i yimenɣi deg imaɣlayen ufrizen
acku hattan tebratt seg ṛuma tessusen as belli tamnaḍt n numidya tattwafka i maryus yella ygza yagi belli aneggaru agi yettwasmel d aqenṣul
asali agi iɣebba t iffer it deg tsusmi d talqayent
yuɣal ur isell ara la tanellayt wala insayen ur yessin ara ad yeṭṭef la imeṭṭawen is wala iles is argaz agi bu tmecfit bu tsertut ifazen yuɣal ur yezmir ara ad ibibb aniri ines
kra rran axuyen agi ɣer tizzengert is kra rran t ɣer tiɣawt iḥulfa yess yiman d amalaɣ deffir tlekkawt ur nettwaklal ara
tuggett seg wurfan n tmeẓṛiwt n trennawt yenneḍṛan
si tura ad as yettwakkes deg wayen i yirzan si tama w ad d snetmeɣ mebla aglugel yettnukmay ɣef usmil n maryus ugar n wakken yennukma ɣef tkennawt i t iḥazen
ad as yufsus uɣilif amer tamnaḍt i as yettwakksen tettwafka i wemdan nniḍen menɣir maryus
ɛewwqen t wumran ɣef umahil u yeẓṛa nnig wayen nni belli d tiɛuggent ad iger iman is deg wayen ur t nerzi werǧin
yuzen s lemɣawla sin imazanen ɣer buixus inɛeṛ as ur yettnizid ara am ucengu lmendad n wegdud aṛumani
ɣur s tura talemmiẓt tameddizit i wakken ad yeg yid s tamaqqant n timmidwa d wemsasa ara yifen s waṭas imenɣi
kra n teflest i yessers ɣef iɣallen is yif it ma ur yemseksal ara ɣer wayen yegluglen beddu n imenɣi d ayen ilemden maca d ayen ileɣten ad as yuqem wemdan talast
mačči d igad d ibeddun imenɣi i yettizmiren dima ad t ssensen beddu s zemren as medden ula d imazdalen ma d asbedi s ɣer waqqas n trennawt
yessefk ihi ɣef bukus ad yenẓeḍ am wergaz amegzu d icellɛan s tɣeḍwifin ines s tid n tgelda s ad yerr dehn is ur iteqqenara tuɣult is yeǧǧuǧugen ɣer tin n yugurten yedren war tadala ɣef tmazaɣin agi yerra d ugellid s wawal aneqqin amasaɣ acemma yebɣa tammazalt maca yemmesmula ɣef tkesniwin n yugurten ma fkan i wegdud agi tiwtal i as fkan ad yilmiḍ wemtawa ɣef yal tineqqiḍin
ɣef tririt agi yuzen unebbaḍ i buxus isumar nniḍen idegga ugellid kra deg sent u yugi tiyaḍ
s wakka i yezri wakud s isumar d isumar imengalen
imenɣi am wakken yebɣa mitilus yettwazmegger ar yifeḍ
maryus yuɣ lḥal yettwafren am akken t id nenna s afella d aqenṣul s lebɣi aḥmayan n wegdud
s imi yeẓṛa belli tamnaḍt n numidya tettwafka yas si tama n wegdud iban d d amekraḍ mgal n iheggaren ugar n zik
di sya d afella yettwellih azwar is tikwal i wusufen tikwal nniḍen i meddan s umata yella yettallas d belli taqensult d arraz n trennawt i d iḥella ɣef iheggaren d yinnawen nniḍen i t yesminigen netta u ssaklalen ten
ɣas akken ur yeǧǧi ara asiteb aheggi i ymenɣi
yessuter s tmerniwt n wemḍan n yemdanen n trebbuyaɛ yak d yegnen inaragen seg yegduden d igelliden d yemsisan yeɣra seg llatyum iyserdasen at tebɣest
yessen tuggett deg sen i ymehlen ddaw tenbaḍt is
kra s yisem nsen mucaɛen deg wakken yetthettit yessenza imsenɣan yettwaserrḥen ad ddun yid s
ɣas akken aseqqamu n yemɣaren ttaksanen maryus nezzeh ur zmiren ara ad as agin teɣawsa alammi ufan taḍfi deg uberreḥ ɣer userbeb anasmad acku ɣillen agdud ad yagi ad yeddem imrigen
u tarewla agi ad tesbennen maryus seg yeɣbula i ɣef yettfulliy ad isetti fell as ahmal n wegdud maca anaruz agi ittwabennen imi tugget tella tebɣa ad teddu d maryus
yella yal yiwen iẓeṛṛ iman is si tura ad yuɣal s axxam is yerna iɛebba s yeglafen
yessedha t unaruz s issenfel maryus seg uddus n trebbuyaɛ i wumi yessuli amḍan seg
iserdasenseg waddad amagnu tezmer ad taweḍ di tḍullit ɣer iserdasen
u tebḍa terbaɛt di tallit is ɣef mraw n trebbuyaɛ u tuɣal tgalift d tayunt n imenɣi tagejdant
u tuɣal s way agi deg ideg n takemmict
teqqim tgaluft tettwasuddes seg kraḍ n tkemmicin d sdis n tgalufin
ɣef usentel agi wali ibaɣuṛen nniḍen ggten ur ixuz ara maryus ad asen yessillef di yiwen deg yinawen ines
acku imi d iḥella seg useqqamu n yemɣarenayen yak yessuter imi yectel deg userbeb iɣra d i wegdud ɣer wegraw i wakken ad ten yesmineg u ad icemmet iheggare u ad ten yesseklel
ẓriɣ nezzeh a yiɣermanen belli igad yessuturen deg wen tanabaḍt s umata ima ara tt id ḥellin tettbeddil tikli nsen uqbel ad awḍen ɣur s ttbanen d d izeddganen d iseddiyen mi tt id ḥellan ad ten tafeḍ tteglilizen di leɛgez d ubekkaḍ
deg wayen iyi yerzan ur ttdekkiḍeɣ slid iɣudfen imuta
d ayagi i yexxitren di twuri n uqensul neɣ lebriṭuṛ
tessefk ihi tmerniwt n tissegli d teɣdeft i useddu s
i deg yettekki usuter is
ur ɣaseɣ ara ɣef tnebdadt i d sḍulli fell i teflest nwen asuteb i ymenɣi rnu ɣer tesbaynut i asekmer n madden ɣef tsekkiwt taserdast ur nebɣi ara asmummi nsen asegfer i wussan iǧunsanen d wuffiyen
ayagi yakk di tlemmast n tismin d usegmeḍ d tixazabiyin d tiddas
d agi a yiɣermanen tizziwt taggarmamt nnig waya nessugum mebla ma nettu ma d abarar i nemmuger ma wiyaḍ ad d afen iman nsen ttwamsetnen s teqbeṛ n iẓuṛan nsen s yiseɣ n imenza nsen yesbehaḍen d tezrart n twaculin nsen d inaragen nsen d tuggett n ineḍfaṛen nsen
ma d nekkin s timmad iw ad sserseɣ akk anaruz inu
ulac allal nniḍen n tmastant ɣef yiman iw slid tabɣes inu d tunẓiẓt inu
acku ayen nniḍen ur yesɛi ara tadusi
rnu ɣer wayagi nekk ẓriɣ a yiɣermanen belli timuɣliwin yakk ttwameyyrent d ɣur i
irgazen imegdayen unẓiẓen fkan iyi d afus n tallelt acku tagduda tettarraz seg tiwaltin iw
u ẓṛiɣ belli iheggaren ttganin talemmiẓt iwakken ad neggzen fell i
ihi yessefk ad rnuɣ ussis iwakken ad rreɣ fell awen takṛiṭ u ad smetreɣ tiddas n iheggaren diɣenna tudert ddreɣ seg temziw tesnam iyi yak imihiyen ayen skareɣ s tmaɣzalt zdat ma ḥellaɣ d tadeggit nwen
idd ad ǧǧeɣ ay agi tura a yiɣermanen deffir mi wwiɣ arrag d tidet asemres n tenbaḍt s tmenzalt d ayen ikemren yuɛren ima ara tili tḥeggast d nettat i d timseggeret i westeɛmel n tuluɣt
deg wayen i yi yerzan nekk yesɛeddan tudert iw yakk deg usemres n tuzulin leḥmala n tuzult tuɣal ɣuri d tumast tissnat
tesɣelfem iyi s useddu n imenɣi mgal yugurten ayen yesserfan iheggaren aṭas
snezzegmet s telqay leɛnaya nwen ma ur tebɣim ara ad tuɣalem deg wawal nwen i tuṭṭfa n tiziwt agi neɣ tin i tt irewsen
argaz seg twacult taqburt i yfelsen s isebdaden imenza u d igellil n leqdic ɣef tmurt war turdut simi ara t id tnegges tizziwt agi ad t yeffer leɛqel u ad yehdiddi di taggara ad yeddem yiwen seg wegdud ad as yemmel ayen yessefken fell as
di tilawt tḍeṛṛu deg tuggett n tikal belli win ara d tesbeddem i tenbaḍt ad inadi si tama s ɣef wayeḍnin ar at yesseddun ad t yenbeḍ
ssneɣ diɣenna a yiɣermanen tiliḍ tazwara ad tettwaferneḍ u ad igad yettganin ad awḍen ɣer tqensult iwakken ad bdun ttḍillin ɣer imahilen gar imenza nneɣ d welɣan ɣef inazayen n legrig deg tnaẓurt taserdasit imdanen yettinziden s unegden acku ma tamrest tesɛa kra n tiziwt
