tiliḍ yessefk tesmerseḍ tt s leqdic s uselkem tura a yičermanen semyifet gar yergazen agi imzengaren d wergaz amaynut am nekkini
ayen slan ttalasen as d medden ayen ẓran nekkini ẓriɣ t s wallen iw
sekreɣ t s ufus iw
ayen lemden deg yedlisen nekk lemdeɣ t deg taɣult n imenɣi
fell awen ad tzerfem acu i yifen d awalen neɣ d igiten
ḥeqqṛen tadra laṣel inu tufrirt u nekkini ḥeqqreɣ tanafast nsen rran war taɣda nsen ɣer usamma ɣef akken ẓerren tumast n tmeṭṭi yiwet u d ayla n madden meṛṛa u belli tbɣest d asulfu n tihuggert u belli amer ad nessuter deg imarawen n albitus n bistya anwa wa i yebɣan ad d yefruri seg sen nitni neɣ d nekkini
amek ara tili tririt nsen deg tmezri nwen ma ur llin bɣan ad fken tudert i win yesɛan ugar n tbɣest
ma sɛan iheggaren azref ad iyi lkin ḥeqṛen
yessefk ad gen kif kif d imenza nsen i yellan ur uklalen ara tihhugra nsen mebɣir aruren am nekk
nitni usmen s yiseɣ agi i yis tesserham
ihi yessefk diɣenna ad asmen ɣef umerret iw d takdidt iw d imihi iyi d immugren
imi s wazal agi i d ḥellaɣ aserhu agi tesgufsa ten tizzengert yeddren am akken ssimẓiyen aserhu nwen aserhu uɣur ttazzalen am akken uklalen t d tidet
agul irgazen agi maca tura takriḍt nsen wigad agi nsen meqqeṛ igad agi i yebɣan ad stummnen s sin ibaɣuṛen d warraz n warur rnu ɣer wayagi mi ddmen awal zdat wen neɣ deg wesqamu n yemɣaren ttaččaren imawen s yiseɣ agi ad yessali ddur nsen ccan nsen
nitni ayagi d ugmiḍ maḍi maḍi
summad tella tudert n widak nni d tameqrant d taxatrant simmad tettban d tinnebrert n wigi d tameqqrant
d tagi i d tidet
iseɣ n imenza am usufu i yneggura nsen ur yettaǧǧa ara deg tili imaladen nsen wala tizulin nsen
ur sɛin ara imenza ad neɛṛen ɣur sen ad kazen s wayagi a yiɣermanen maca ay gifen d akken zemreɣ ad mmeslayeɣ ɣef yiseɣ inu s timmad iw
walit i yettzuxxun s arur ur nelli nsen ttagin iyi ayen uklaleɣ s timmad iw war turda acku ur sɛin ara imenza u tihhugra inu d tamaynutt meṛṛa
am akken ur t yif ara ad d tesseɣnuḍ ad d txelqeḍ tihhugra inek s yiman ik wala ad d tekkasid tihhugra n wiyeḍnin u ad tt tessamseḍ
d tidet gziɣ belli ma bɣan tura tiririt ad ṭṭfen aṭas n tebratin yettwaselsen akken iwuta maca imi ɣellten tagnit n userhu ameqqṛan id iyi tefkam iwakken ad iyi d ṣṣeṛwun rregmat di yal adɣar ur ssusmeɣ ara ugadeɣ ad t ɣillen am akken d akaz ala usar nekkin leɣdeɣ nezzeh belli ulac ameslay ara yi kmun ma yella d tidet
d awezɣi ad yili macci d win ara yi smingen
ma yella d akerkas tudert iw tihdi w qudden i wesbugget maca imi d tiɣtasin nwen i yettwajeddaɛen ssugnuten ken imi yi tefkam aserhu ameqqran d tiziwt tazayant
snezzegmet nezzeh iwakken ur tettmugruẓem ara
iwakken ad d ḥelliɣ taflest nwen ur zmireɣ ara ad awen d ssekneɣ iwlalen n trennawin neɣ tiqensulin imenɣa inu maca ma tessutrem d tagnit ad ssekneɣ imrigen n yillafen ladɣa ccamat n waggaṣen iyi ḥazen meṛṛa s zzat
d tigi i d iwlafen inu d wigi i d isental n yiseɣ iw ur ten id sgerweɣ ara seg wakkasu am nitni maca rebḥɣ ten s ugemmer n tudert iw
imeslayen iw war tazuri rnu ɣer wayagi ur d cliɛeɣ ara tuzult tettbeggin d iman is
nitni ṣran i tiɛɛubja deg yinnawen iwakken ad izmiren ad ffren tinnebrert nsen
ur zriweɣ ara tasekla n legrig ur bɣiɣ werǧin tazrawt ur nettherrig ara i yinelmaden is leḥmala n tuẓult
ayen ɣriɣ d netta i yugaren yidaf n tigduda lemdeɣ ad wteɣ acengu ad mmestaneɣ ɣef teqcelt iwakken ur ttagadeɣ kra slid akacaf
ad zzidreɣ i weẓɣal d teṣmeḍ kif kif ad ṭseɣ ɣer lqaɛa srid ad zzidreɣ i laẓ d tremmuyt d tigi i d timsirin ttakeɣ i yserdasen iw ur ttḥettimeɣ ara fell asen anɣud u nekkini steɛfaɣ
ur bennuɣ ara tarennawt inu ɣef lmerta nsen
yessefk ad yenbeḍ win d ilhan s teɣdeft n tmurt d yegmir n yeɣermanen
ma netta itedder di leɛgez u ad yesseklel i yal lmerta igen ines
tagi d tikli nusnaraf mačči d tin unabbaḍ s uselkam tizebgatin d yiwen warraz aserdasan tekṣa seg tkurin ttimeẓayanin n ureɣ neɣ n lfeṭṭayettwagal di temgerṭ neɣ tettwaskan d ɣef teɣzi n tziba imenzayen agi ṣkan n imenza nwen addur nsen d trennawt n tegduda sbeɣṛen iheggaren seg yigazen agi imeqqṛanen uɣur ttaken anzi ciṭuḥ kan ur aɣ ttagaden ara nekni yettemdeggaren yid sen u ssuturen deg wen yal timanagin mačči am warraz d ittuḥellayen
maca am warraz d azref nsen
ah acḥal ttagalen yergazen agi imzengaren
ǧǧan asen d imenza nsen kra n wayen iwumi zemren ad t id ǧǧen tabaɣurt iwlafen aktayen aktayen iminag maca ur asen seksan ara tuẓulin nsen
ur zmiren ara
d yiwen wayla i wer nezmir la ad t nefk wala ad aɣ ittwanefk
qqaren belli ur ssineɣ acemma di tmeɣriwin u belli ur sɛiɣ ara agunnactal wala amnawel a yi d yesqam nnig tefniɣin inu
ay agi ad t deggiɣ u ad zuxxeɣ yes s acku lemdeɣ ɣef baba d wudmawen nniḍen d unẓiẓen tasrifa d amur n tlawin u amahil d amzday n yergazen tamanegt di tmuɣli n wergaz yuklalen isem agi d tabaɣurt imrigen is d nitni i yessiliɣen tasrifa ines mačči d ifecka ines
ihi yelha ad kemmlen ayen ḥemmlen imi ɣlay fell asen ad gnen idd tilawin ad sekṛen ad sɛeddin tewser nsen anda sɛeddan temẓi nsen deg wučči d tissit d zzhu d aklan iɛebbaḍ nsen d yigman inezfuyen ad aɣ ǧǧen inekni tidi d uɣebbaṛ d wayen nniḍen i nferren ɣef temsist nsen maca ala deffir mi ttwakecfen s inurifen agi yak
ad d asen wudmawen iǧǧiden agi yak ad ḥewṣen adduren uzrifen n yemdanen imalaɣen
ayagi ad yernu ɣer tekriḍt d wehyad abekkaḍ d leɛgez yugaren yakk ibekkaḍen deg webdil n tyita n yigad yesskaren annect a sseɣḍalen tagduda ur ngi kra ubekkaḍ
tura imi asen d sgedleɣ akken i t teswar tumast iw mačči am akken bɣan
ad awen d iniɣ kra n wawalen ɣef waddad zdat yalac ɣef numidya ur seɛɛut ara anezgum a yiɣermanen acku ayen yellan yettallan yugurten ar tura temɣer uɛebbuḍ aɛgaz zzux tesguggemt
rnu ɣer wayagi tesɛam dinna igen yessen tamurt
maca d tidet yella yesɛa ugar n tebɣest wala tlemmizin acku yella tɣurr it temɣer uɛebbuḍ d temseksalt n inebbaḍen is
kunwi yewwḍen awtay n userbeb rnut d ussis nwen ɣer wussis inu yyaw ɣer leqdic ɣef tegduda ur ttkukrut ara seg tiggucert n yemdukal nwen neɣ tizzengert n inebbaḍen ad iliɣ s timmad iw yid wen di tikli am wakken tḍeṛṛu deg imenɣi ad ken seɣdeɣ ad zdiɣ ɣer tama nwen deg imahiyen nwen ula d tamezla gar i yid wen ayen i ɣef ad awen in snetmeɣ d akken s tallalt n iṛebbiwen yal imadden lɣellat n imenɣiyen nezzen tarennawt iglafen taminegt ɣas ma tella deg s turdut neɣ teggugyessefk ɣef yal yiwen d akannaw ad yazzel s lemɣawla ad yessilel tagduda azdal werǧin yesgugg tamettant ɣef yiwen
ulac ababat yessaramen taɣilalt tudert n ugemmir d tuzult
ad d iniɣ ugar a yiɣermanen amer i warraw is maca yessaram asen imeslayen ssembawalen ulawen n imezdal i yinebɣasen ɣilleɣ nniɣ d ayen ara yqudden deffir yinnaw agi i yebɣa maryus ad ifaṛeṣ anafag n wegdud iɣawel iɛebba addur lmuna d tiɣraḍ n iserdasen d yemrigen yal icermaḍ inheḍ s tallalt i inyus manilyus s tiddin idd taɣlamt imi yella netta yesserbeb tigulaf mačči am tnamiyin tiqbuṛin neɣ s tarrayt tadilant meɛna s weqbal n imaɣzalen imɣad
yella userbeb alammi d tallit n maryus iḍeṛṛu deg agens n tsartutin tinkalwiyin i gzemren ad tesserbeb iman is maca deg tallit n maryus d afella idarren n tserdast llin i yal iɣermanen
u yuɣal userbeb ɣef tmasit n uwanek
igad yettwasguggen seg umeẓlu tugget deg sen am akken ẓeṛṛen d tanuṭṭaft n tilawt n wid ten yifen wiyiḍ ẓeṛṛen d tanuttaft n tẓitla uqensul i timinegt ines
d wigi i tt yeṣkan di tillawt
argaz yettnadin ɣef tenbaḍt ineḍfaren yelhan d wid yelluẓen ugar ulac di tmuɣli nsen kra n wayen yesɛan azal kra n wayen ara sen d iḥellin ciṭuḥ ɣur sen yesserhuy
iṛuḥ ihi maryus ɣer ifriqya ddant yid s kra n tgalufin amḍan nsen iɛedda ayen yettuseklen deg teɣtast n userbeb
ires deffir n kra n wussan di weftas n ɛutiqa
yeṭṭef tanbaḍt seg ufus n unarag bibyus sṛutilyus acku militus yessunef maryus i wakken ur yettili ara d inigi n tedyant
mačči kan ur yezmir ara ad yessefrek
deffir mi yessemda uqunsul tirebbuyaɛ d usali ines tigalufin ines tinarigin yuheẓ di tmurt d tablalast u d tanebɣuṛt s igulaf
ayen yakk ara ykewwec yettaǧǧa t i yserdasen yuzeɣ tiɣermin tinamumin ur nelɣit ara s ugama
tid yesɛan drus n tmastanin
yekcem deg imenɣiyen deg waṭas n idigen maca d tifessasin
iserdasen imaynuten s wakka ad nnamen war tuggdin imenɣiyen
ad ẓṛen imerwal ad nɣen ad skerfen u belli inebɣasen d nitni i ɣef d iɣelli drus n imihi u belli imrigen ttwasrasen i tmastant ɣef tlelli d tmurt d imarawen yak d wiyaḍ meṛṛa taggara
am akken d issegluy s tminegt d tbaɣurt
akka dɣa fsin iserdasen imaynuten deg yeqbuṛen u tuɣal tebɣes tugda ɣer sen yakk
ma d ayen yerzan sin nni ineglusen ddirzen bih bih simi ẓṛan yewweḍ d maryus yal yiwen si tama s di temnaḍin ttwassnent
diɣenna yeɣtes yugurten iɛewwel u yessarem ur yettɛeṭṭil ara ad inbeḍ ɣef ucengu yemmezren simi ara yennefsusi ṛṛuman ɣef weɣyud am akken iḍeṛṛu di tnammit imi ara tṛuḥ fell asen tuggdi
imir nni yella mitilus iṛuḥ yagi ɣer ṛuma mmugren t id nemgal n wayen yella yettgani s tdawit d tanafagt
yeɣba ukasan
aɛuzzu sed yekkan ɣur wegdud ur yelli ara d unkiẓ ɣef win useqqamu n yemɣaren deg wayen yerzan maryus iga ɣef terbaɛt is taggaẓt am akken t iga ɣef ucengu taggaẓt turmudt tamḥarebt
izerrew tineqqdin n tdusi n tid n tumunt
di sin yegnen yettgani amussu n sin igelliden yessenṭaṛ tiddan n igunad nsen
yeǧǧa iserdasen ines zgan deg usmuteg u wiyeḍnin deg umennuɣǧef
s wakka i yuzeɛ yugurten d iǧitulen u yeẓṛa ten yuɣal d s wagga n igelfan i d yehwes i yemsasayen ines
ula deg yideg yusen ɣer qirṭa izzelmami agellid ad isres tarbabt is
maca yegza belli ma tirennawin agi ttawint as d taminegt maca ur d ttawint ara tifrat
iɣtes ad yessutel s temlellit tindin i ahat ad weɛṣent s yideg agmawi neɣ s tmastant nsent
ama ad ifḍen yugurten seg tallalt ma yeǧǧa t ad yeg ama ad yettwazemlelli ɣef imenɣi
ma d buxus yella yettazen as d i maryus belli yebɣa ad tili timidawit ger asen d wegdud aṛumani u belli ur yesɛi ara yaǧad si tama s
wissen ayenni ma yella d tiddest iwakken ad aɣ d yuzeɣ s taẓwayt neɣ d agmuḍ n tibbehnest i t yettdeggiren tikwal ɣer tammazalt u tikwal ɣer imenɣi
mačči d ayen ilemḍen i tigzi
akka dɣa i yuzeɣ uqensul timdinin am akken yeɣtes yakk d tɣermiwin ileɣten ismares ad ten yebḍu s yiɣil u tikwal s uṛeggem neɣ s usiged
di tazwara iga kan kra n teskar
yefles belli yugurten ad d yasu ad ifeki afus n tallalt i yneḍfaṛen ines maca mi yegza belli yugurten yeggug u yelha d d iweẓla nniḍen yufa belli yessefk ad yeg kra n tsekkirin yesɛan ugar n tixxutra d uɣennej
tella di tlemmast n tneẓruft yiwet n temdint d tameqqrant d tamedwart qqaren as gefṣa issenta tt ɣef akken d qqaṛen herqel alibi imezdaɣ is ttwasurfen deg tikci n tbezzart
yettemyag yid sen yugurten s waṭas n lemqadṛa
ɣef way agi llan d imidwiyen yid s aṭas
tella di talfast seg wanbazen n icenga
mačči kan si tilɣi n yeɣraben ines d tadusi n igadiren ines d wemḍan n iɣallen ines kan maca diɣenna s uganaḍ s luɛaṛa n yideg wideg d zga
acku slid iglagalen d yuẓen ɣer temdint
ayen d iqqimen yak d taneẓṛuft war azraɛ wala aman teččuṛ d izerman i yrennun tiqqujṛa
akken iḍeṛṛu di lebda d iɣeṛsiwen micki ur ufin ara d acu ara ččen
mebla ma nettu belli izerman ttuɣalen d imihiyen ugar micki fuden
yella maryus yebɣa nezzeh ad ikewwec gefṣa ama i tixxutra ines i ymenɣi i yilɣi n tamsaksalt d tminegt i d iḥella mitilus mi ikewwec tala wer nemmeẓli deg waddad ines deg tnezmarin n tmastant
deg s slid belli gefṣatama n ugafa n tafrawt n yugurten
deg s i rsen ibaynuten is akken i d inna strabun
yettwafka yisem n heṛqel i waṭas n wudmawen umyisen deffir heṛqel agrigi i ten yugren addur
didru n siqilliya tlata d cicrun seta d faru tnin uṛebɛin
i wmezdaɣ di tala yuɣ llan kra n yeɣbula ur negugg ara ɣef iɣurban
ma di gefṣa ulac slid yiwet n tala trttceṛcuṛ u deg gens n temdint i tella iwakken ad semmden ankaẓ ttuɣalen ɣer waman n ugeffur
u ad nesmaw s umsenyif dagi am akken yella waddad di yal tamiwin n friqya yegguggen ɣef yill
tudert tuɣ tezga d taqurart
ankaẓ agi n waman ur yessileɣ ara afḍam ameqqran imi inumidiyen yenqedwa ad ččen war ayefki d ikusman n wegmar war asemres n tisent neɣ ayen nniḍen yettaken adurdu učči ɣur sen yettwag i wesrusu n laẓ d fad
ur ẓerren ara deg s allal n ustummen d ubekkaḍ
ihi deffir mi yessegra uqensul yalec ibda amahil ifulla ɣef tallalt n iṛebbiten iwakken ad frun ilɣiten d ittbanen weɛṣen ɣef tezmart n yemdanen iman nsen
terna d inumidiyen yettakentixxutra ugar i isuyas n tyessawt ɣef tyerza n yirden
rnu ɣer wayenni tuɣ wwin d ɣer temdint yettwaleɣten ciṭuḥ nni n lɣella ammad iɣiṛ ssawḍen ad t id gerwen s uniẓeḍ n yugurten
imi anebdu yuẓ d ifak agama imir nni yella yeqquṛ u yuzzef yak ulamma aqensul iluɛeǧ yalec s tmazeɣt yessefken u s tasmakta i yes yessuref umaɣlay
inẓed imnayen imaragen ad nehṛen lmal i d ssuksen deg ussan yezrin
yuzen amarag ines inyus manilyus idd iterrasen fessusen ɣer laras tamdint i deg llant teɣraḍ n yigen d waddur n twaɣit n wenkaẓ n waddur nneɛma yessisen as ad t iqḍeɛ deffir n kra n wussan
deffir n tḥeggast n temnaḍt iffer s wayagi tidmi ines yuẓ ɣer wasif n tanayes
di tegnit nni n tikli yella yessedgar yal ass i yigen ines imuren yemmegḍan n lmam i lmend n tiyunin timiḍiwin d tgalufin llan ttagen deg yilwan nsent ticulliḍin issunef s wayagi ankaẓ n imendi yettheggi diɣen ayen ara yuser war asisen n yiwen imi wwḍen deffir setta n wussan ɣer wasif
yella wemdan ameqqṛan n tculliḍin ihegga
dinna dɣa issenta tiqcelt is i yefreg afrag afessas
inẓeḍ iserdasen ad ččen
d wesmuteg i tikli mi yeɣli yiṭiǧ u ad ǧǧen yak icermaḍen d lehwayec n waggay slid wid yettawin aman
mi yeẓṛa yewweḍ d wakkud yeffeɣ seg teqcelt ur yebdid ara alammi yelḥa ka yekka yiḍ yerna akkenni iḍ i d iḍefṛen iḍ wi kraḍ zdat tafrara yewweḍ ɣer temnaḍt ttabudrart teggug ma aṭas sin imilen ɣer gefṣa dinna yeffer ayen iwumi yezmer netta d yigen ines yak yeqqim yegguni imi d yuli wass ffɣen d inumidiyen seg temdint d tirebbuyaɛ yella wayen ugaden war turda imir nni inẓeḍ uqensul s tuzwayt yal iserdasen is d iterrasen is ass agi asif n dderb d asif yezgan ileḥḥu itekk lewhi n ɣef gafṣa
wali gsell
asb
tayunt tumidit d tayunt taserdasit neɣ tanedbalt taṛumanit taqbuṛt yudes s yemdanen yessedduy itt unabaḍ n miyya
tḍac ten yessummulen yettɣawalen ugar iwakken ad zerbentaɣda n gefsa d ukemmec n tebbura irna ɣur sen s timmad is s urured d urmud war ma yessuref i yiserdasen s theggaṣt
gzan imezdaɣ amihi tmuɣli nsen tuggdi rrebrab tiddehcert mi ẓṛan iɣeṛman nsen deg uffuɣ n temdint n igadiren nnekmaren i wannuz
ɣas akken ur temniɛ ara temdint seg uṣerɣi d tmenɣiwt n yal inumidiyen yebbḍen taggaṭ
ttwazenzen wiyaḍ d aklan teyywabḍa teglaft ɣef iserdasen
tigawt agi i yemmeẓlen d izerfan n imenɣi ur d teswawi ara i wqenṣul
ur iḥḥulfa la s temɣer uɛebbuḍ wala s tiẓẓuḍt maca tamdint tenfeɛ i yugurten tettwafreg imezdaɣ imtettiyen imnegdamen imakrasen weɛsen i temsirt ar yimir nni la s yiɣil wala s tulluɣt
deffir aseḍru n trennawin agi war ma yesṛuḥ ula d yiwen wergaz
iban d maryus i yesɛan addur meqqer umayna
ugar addur d temɣer tura ula d isenfaren ines mseksalen ugar llan ttbanen d am tteḥfat tiserdasin
tamyagawt d iserdasen ines s tmaqqunt tikci n tlemmiẓt iwakken ad sɛun abaɣur ayagi idegger iten ad t ssalin ɣer tqacuct
inumidiyen llan ttagaden t am wemdan iffɣen i tnumi
meṛṛa yiwen wawal imsasayen icenga ɣilen t yesɛa tadusi tarebbanit mawlac neɣ d win iẓeṛṛen imal s lebɣi d waqqas n rebbi
deffir trennawt agi inṭeg ɣef temdint nniḍen izzemlelli amḍan ameẓyan n temdinin i deg rran inumidiyen u yeṣṣreɣ tugget n temdinin i deg rran inumidiyen u yeṣṣreɣ tugget n temdinin i deg guǧǧen imezdaɣ deffir imi slan s twaɣit n gefṣa teɣli d tmettant d wumran di yal ideg deffir mi ikemmec aṭas n idigen tugget war ma yessenɣel tiqqit idammen iṛumaniyen
iɣtes ɣef tɣawsa nniḍen war nesɛi ara iswaɣ i tesɛa gefṣa ulamma ur telli ara mebla ilɣitan ur yeggug ara ɣef wasi n malawiya i yebḍan tagelda n yugurten d buxus
tuɣ yella di tlemmast n tmurt d luḍa adrar d aẓru yuli aṭas ulac talluyt ɣur s slid ɣef yiwen usaka d ukmir yal ayen d iqqimen yettwanjeṛ d agmawi seg waẓṛu yettban d am akken d afus n wedan i t yeṣkan
iɣtes maryus ad d iḥelli tiɣremt agi s yiɣil imi deg s ayedda n ugellid maca deggimi tbedd ɣef twenza ugar tanaḍt yella waṭas n terbabt aṭas n yergazen tamuḍ tameqqrant n yirden yak d tala n waman yuzzlen yella yideg ur yettwahegga ara i tigawt n yiḥfiren d lebraǧ
yiwen webrid i yettawin ɣer yeɣṛem d ukmir nezzeh yettfaka s yiran ssegrarben aṭas
cimi ara taẓeḍ cituḥ ad t ṛzen imessutal s tmes neɣ s yeẓṛa
tilɣi n taɣult ur tessuref ara i yiserdasen la s iɣimi zdat tmeṣkiwin nsen wala anduddi ddaw tiyita n yillan
at tebɣest tameqqrant ttwaɣen neɣ ttwaggsen
ɣur wiyaḍ yella rrebrab yettnerni yal ass
imenɣi yeẓṛa deffir mi izella maryus ussan d wusan d imeqqranen
yesteqsa iman is s kra unuɣni ma ad yeǧǧ asenfar nni ideg iẓeṛṛ abarar neɣ ad yeggani ẓẓheṛ i yennumen yettebdad ɣer tama s
yuɣ lḥal yesɛedda ussan d wuḍan deg uzamma yagi ugṛiḥ war ma yewweḍ ɣer tefrat imi d yeffeɣ seg teqcelt yiwen userdas aquri d amagnu seg tgaluft tamaragt deg uɛezzer iwakken ad yawi aman u yeẓṛa ɣef yidis n wedrar ugemmaḍ n temnaḍt iɛaṛusen yetteḥnunufen gar tezrutin
yelqeḍ d yiwen sin tugget war ma iḥulfa deg tibbekt alammi yewweḍ qrib ɣer tqacuct n wedrar dinna yeẓṛa belli ula ula d yiwen yunez imir nni i taggayt agi tawnafit tagnugt yesɛa wemdan i t ittdeggiren di lebda ad d iḥelli timinag
ayagi yeswawi yas d asenfar nniḍen
yella d inna useklu ubelluḍ d ameqqran igma gar teẓṛa tella tazwara d agussar yettwaɣed zzeg s akin u yegma d asawen am akken gemmen meṛṛa yemɣan
alliguri agi yetter tallalt n ifurkan tikwal tikwal nniḍen s ifuden n teẓra
alammi yewweḍ ɣer wazuɣ n teɣremt war ilɣiten acku ur d lhin ara inumidiyen ala s imenɣi i ten iggunin la iḍeṛṛun deffir mi yani yal idigen deg usugen is tarmit agi ines ahat ad a ten texdem dṛuɣ
yuɣal d am wakken yuli maca mačči am akken yuli gedd gedd meɛna s wakaz n lqaɛa ismaw yalac iṛuḥ imir imir ad yemlil maryus iwakken ad as yessegzi ɣef yal tamsaksalt ines yelɣa yas ad yeg tarmit si tama i deg yuli issers iman is ddaw ufus i tawalt d amnir u ad iṭawel iman is d amezwaru yuzen maryus idd lliquri tekna acemma tdeggirt is imahiyen iwselken seg kra imeslayen is u wigini sgelmen as taɣawsa agi am akken d talemmadt neɣ d tukmirt guncek tumast nsen ɣas akken tuɣal as d i uqunṣul ciṭuḥ n teflest
yeffren ger yigad yettṣuḍun di lbuq d yegad yettṣuḍun deg wacciwen semmus deg wid fessusenn d kuẓ seg iɣellaten n tmiḍi inẓḍ iten meṛṛa ad aɣen awal n lliquri
yesguccel d azekka nni i wselkem n temhelt timuggit
deg wakud yettwasbedden yalec yella yettwahegga yettwasuddes yuɣ d lliguri ɣer wedɣar yettwafernen
llan yagi wid yulinsmesseklen beddlen imrigen nsen talusi nsen am akken sen yenna umnir nsen
iqurray d iḍarren nsen uzfen iwakken ad ẓṛen ttif w ad ckenṭḍen di teẓṛa ttif u s tillunḍa ugar
llan gan igestulen d tiziba ɣef yeɛrar nsen tiziba n weglim am tziba n iumidiyen iwakken ad ifsisen fell asen wad yeswawi wemyegges nsent ẓdiḥ udris yezwar lliguru di yal wanda llant teẓṛa neɣ iẓuṛan iqbuṛen yesɛan ifuden
iteqqen imurar ara yalalen imdukal is ad yessigel fell asen micki ten yessaged usegrarab nwemdiq u ad as ifek afus n tallalt imi ara yili usegrarab yeɛkeṛ itekkes fell asen imrigen u ad ten yugaẓ s timmad is u ad ten yerr tekken zdat s yiwen yiwen ima ara d mmagren aṣuk i ɣef ulac taflast aṭas ad iɛeddi d amezwaru i wenkad n yideg
yettali yettader aṭas n tikkal zzeg s akin ad ten yeǧǧ ad ɛeddin di teflest taggara
deffir lmerta d wussis wwḍen ɣer wazuɣ si tama tajulbit acku inumidiyen ttmagaren acengu si tama tagummaḍt am wussan yezrin
yettwalɣet maryus s webrid n yemcegɛen s usemres n tizziwt n lliquri ulamma yennuɣ imenɣi azaccal teɣzi n wass yefka isebɣasen imaynuten i yigen is
yuẓ s timmad is yemla yasen amek ara ssudsen icermaḍ imenɣi allalen aɛrur n yefker s wakka yuẓ ɣer udasil n yeɣraben di lawan i deg icermaḍen n imenɣi d yiddad yekkaten s ikuffa d wid yekkaten s yillawen zzuzuren arebreb seg wuggug deg idarren n ucengu inumidiyen snegdamen neɣ sserɣayen icermaḍ nneɣ ur ffiren ara iman nsen deffir i iɣurban maca ttganin assa d yiḍ ɣef yiri n uɣrab ugadir ttargamen ṛṛuman zzawaren maryus ɣef yisiḍ isssumulen iserdasen is s uṣeklelli
s wakka yerra ten usemres nneɣ d uqbiḥen di tegnit i deg icenga yak deg tegnitt n imenɣi d izaccalen si snat n tamiwin kra ilmend n trennawt d timmuqra n tegduda ma d wiyaḍ ifker d tamuddut tella tettwasemras deg igen aṛumani s usdarri n iserdasen wa deffir wa mẓeyyaṛen tizwa nsen nnig igerray nsen sselɣayen s wayen nni ayen yettaken anzi ɣer teɛrurt n yefker ayen i asen yessurfen ad beddan ddaw yeɣraben n udasil yettwasutlen u ad alin wa deffir wa iwakken ad awḍen ɣer tqacuct di lawan i deg kkaten at ikuffa d at yillan s ineccaben d yeẓṛa ɣef ucengu
ilmend n tudert nsen tetterdeq s tuẓwayt taɣuct n lbuq s deffir llant tlawin d imezyanen i d yenzeɣ ẓẓdiḥ d tawnafit rewlen rnan wid yellan uẓen d ɣer ugadir
taggara rewlen yak imsenɣan d wiyaḍ di temmarwayt agi iṛṛumaniyen rnan tadwast n wussis nsen ṭṭafaren imerwalen s wenɣud ikumren ugar ttaǧǧan imyaggaṣen mebla ma kemmlen asen zeggren ɣef inegzamen d tazzla ɣer tmanegt uɣur fuden ttemḥizwiren
anwa ara yawḍen d amezwaru ɣer iɣerban meṛṛa bɣan taheggast
s wakka ay yessewken usamma tamsaksalt n maṛyus ay yufan deg wagul ay iga talemmiẓt i tmmegt
imir nni yewweḍ usefrak lukyus ɣer teqcelt
ddan d yid s aṭas n yemnayen yettwasrebben
imi asentel yebder aɣ d argaz anemɣur iban aɣ d deg webdar a ad d nini kra n wawalen ɣef tawgidt d tumast ines deg tilawt ulac deg tedmi nneɣ ad d naru anezgum n sula deg yiden niḍen
seg tama niḍen luky sizina ula ma d yuɛer ad yefles yiwen belli mraw n yergazen semmus deg sen widak yettsuḍun di lbuqat d wacciwen d ṛebɛa n inabbaḍen n tmiḍin d lliguri ad ssekren rrebrab agi yak u ad kewwcen iɣṛem
ula d fruntinyus d ibedren adris n salustyus yenna d ay agi ulamma ur d iferreh ara amḍan n inabbaḍen n tmiḍin yerna ɣur sen amḍan seg iserdasen urmiden ugar
sizina lukyus kurnilius dat sɛ d argaz n tsertit d tsekla yettwasmel d asefrak deg siqilya aseggas n dat sɛ sakkin d abriṭur deg axayus
yebda s tira n yimenɣi n numas deg tewser is yessuffeɣ d taceqquft n umezgun n wemduddi n temdint ay d tufut d usdid wid ay d yemmeslayen ɣef tikli is ur d mmeslayen ara dima ɣef wakken ay ttwaliɣ s uzagur uqqid
lukyus sula seg twacult tugrigt maca seg yiwen n ufurk qrib yettwattun
s weɛgaz n yimenza ines usliden yella d bab n tussna tulqayt s tsekliwin tigrigiyin d tlatiniyin d bab n tzitla tuhriwt
yella iḥemmel zzhu maca tamanegt ugar
ma yella yesɛedday akud n usṭurres deg uhegges ɣas ula ma aya ur as yessutuy ara taɣudfin is slid tudert ines tanaragt yella yezmer ad yerkawel s tudert tamekdit ugar d asreqqa d aɣafad d ushil n tmidawit d akukmi drus am netta deg waya
d azenzar deg yalec ula deg yidrimen is ula ma yella yugar akk irgazen deg tumert sdat n ternawt is
deg umennuɣ aɣarim maca tawensa ines ur telli ara nnig n wayen yuklal
mačči d yiwen ay yesseqsan iman is
ma d tabɣest is tugar tumert is kan
ma d ayen ay iga seg s akkin ur d qqareɣ acemma i lmend n tiddurit leḥya d yiniri leḥzen
yeswawi ubellen ay yeḍran gar maṛyus d sula ɣef wazal n yiweẓla imahilen izerfanen
wali cicrun brutus
tawacult d afurk seg wedrum neɣ tamedla
afurk n kurnulyus aydeg yella sula
yella yagi yuder u yers wazal is i lmend n uxuyen n yimenza is usriden
ur ɛeddan ara i tnawurt n tenbaḍt
yiwen seg sen ur yewwiḍ ɣer tqenṣult
mi yewweḍ sula ɣer friqiya d yemnayen is ur iṛuḥ ɣer teqcelt n maṛyus am wakken ay d nenna sufella
ur yelli yesɛa la tarmit wala tussna ɣef yimenɣi u deg wakud d awezlan yuɣal yugar iten meṛṛa deg tiddenkit nnig waya yella d aẓil mnid yiserdasen yettarra d awal i yiserdasen u iqeḍḍu asen d lebɣi nsen sdat ma ssutren t id
ur yettdeggi ara ur iqebbel tawalin ala s wesmummi yerna yettɣawal ad ten id yerr am wakken d amerwas
ur yessutur acemma ɣer yiwen
werǧin yettnadi d anagar ad d iḥelli ayen umi yezmer deg yigar umi ara yettalas
yessen amek ara imeɛɛek deg ugella ula netta d imanzalen nezzeh yezga yettekkay deg yimahilen timsekniyin aɛezzeṛ rnu werǧin ad ijedder addur n uqenṣul neɣ argaz niḍen ay yesɛan azal am wakken sskaren deg tnamit imaztalen ur yesɛin ara tiddenkit
yezga yettnadi akken ur yettili ara yenkeẓ ɣef la deg useqqamu wala deg umahil nnig yiwen yiṛumaniyen a akk
tikliwin a rrant t yesɛa azal ɣer maṛyus d yiserdasen
yuɣ lḥal deffir mi yeṛǧeḥ yugurten gefsa d temdinin niḍen ileɣten u xutrent amur niḍen ixuter deg tesbaynut is yuzen i buxus yeɣra as ad yesseddu iɣallen is s lemɣawla ɣer numidya yewweḍ wakud n yimenɣi gziɣ dakken buxus yella yettgelgal u yella yessemḍan aruren n tmazzalt d yimenɣi war ma yessaweḍ ɣer teɣtast
yules yugurten i wenduddu amezwaru yesgufsa isefkan imwaẓiyen n ugellid
iṛeggem i ugellid s timmad nnes s wezgen n numidya ma ttwaẓẓɛen yiṛumaniyen seg friqiya neɣ ma yessenked as umsasa n tammazalt azlaɣ n tmurt is
yenẓa buxus s uṛeggem a u yeqḍeɛ yugurten s waṭas n yergazen
simi mgarawen yignen nsen nebzen maṛyus ay yellan yetteddu ɣer tsegrast ines neṭgen fell as deg wakud n wass aydeg ur d yeqqim slid tis mraw deg umanad nsen belli iḍ ay d yetteddun ad ten yemmesten ma d tirẓi ay ten yeggunin acemma ur ten yeswaɣay ma wwin tarennawt imi ay ssnen tamurt d anemgal deg wayen yerzan ṛṛuman
akken yebɣu yili yiḍ ad ten yessers deg yir tagnit
akka ihi deg tegnit aydeg ssisnen maṛyus seg yal tamiwin dakken acengu la d yetteddun aneggaru a yella sdat s sdat ma yuddes yigen i yimenɣi neɣ assegrew n yicermad u sdat n tuḍḍfa n kan tamuli neɣ kra tanaḍt
neṭgen yemnayen imuriṭaniyen i yimenɣi wala i kra n tillit maca deg trebbuyaɛ ttwassuddsent s usamma ccil aberwi d yeswawi unṭag a ameẓway
ṛṛuman ur ttun ara tabɣest nsen kra n wwin imrigen nsen neɣ mmestanen ɣef yimeddukal nsen ay d yelhan s usebeb kra unan rekben igmaren ṛuḥen ad mmagren acengu yewwi yimenɣi timeẓrit n tḥeggaṣt ugar tin n illafen mmerwin yimenɣi usdis war yemnayen d yiterrasen kra ddirzen kra mmenɣen aṭas seg sen zzemlelli acengu ad ten yemmager tiririt tella d tazacalt maca ufan d iman nsen s tuẓwayt ttwasetlen s deffir
imrigen tabɣest llan ɣur sen tarennawt s wemḍan nnezwin deg yal adɣar taggar ṣkan yemsenɣan iqburen d yimaynuten tiẓuyar deg yal adɣar anda ay ten id yessegrew wedɣar n asama
s tulluɣ n tmuddut a ssawḍen ad mmestanen yerna ad rren ɣef yal tamiwin wwin ddeṛk war tirriza i tenṭagin n ucengu
deg waddad a ukmir ur yesṛuḥ ara maṛyus la tesmeḍ n yidammen is wala tabɣest is ɣef uqerruy n terbaɛt seg yinḍafen is ay yessuddes seg wid yugaren akk tebɣest deg weɣram n yimeddukal is wiyaḍ deg imiḍwiyen yella yettaɣ d ɣer yal tamiwin
tikkwal yettakf tallalt i wid yeddirizen tikkwal yettazeɣ acengu ixuyen deg tlemmast n anda ttdarran s umyuṭṭeɛ temterwit tamatut anda ay yessaweḍ imizden ines i yiserdasen is
u yebɣa ihi ma ulac ad ten yellel s yiɣallen ines
tura ass yezri war ma tenkeẓ tekriḍt n lberber mmenẓen s temrit n ugellid nsen dakken iḍ iqeddec i ubaɣur nsen
gar ugar n wussis i tuẓẓɛa nneɣ
imir nni yegza maṛyus tilawt i wakken ara yessenked arigez i yigen ines yeḍḍef snat n tɣalltin myuddasent yiwet tekmer i tmeṣkiwt n teqcelt deg s tala tettmar tis snat tesɛa adeg iwulmen i ussebded n ugrur acku tella d timinegt aṭas u tessegrareb deg tuget ur d tessutur ara srid kra n usselɣet afessas
yessunneḍ s tiḍaf deg yiḍ tazzin n tala s tiddin n yemnayen is yeslemmeẓ tagnit n temterwit ɣur ucengu ines daɣ yessegrew d cwiṭ n s yiserdasen is sakkin yessedda ten yemmezrin
lemɣawla ɣer tiɣilt tis snat addad n wedɣar yezzelmelli igelliden ad sbedden imenɣi war ma ssurfen i yegnan nsen s tgellawt u gerwen d ignan nsen ɣef snat n tewririn qqimen deg temnaḍt d tameqrant deffir mi ssaɣen timessiwin sɛeddan amur ameqran n yiḍ ttbeyyinen d tadawit nsen s ccḍiḥ nsen d usuɣu s yiwar tinamiyin nsen inabbaḍen nsen ttzuxxun s tizzengert d tanafsast ẓerren iman nsen rnan imir ur rwilen ara
deg tegnit aydeg llan ṛṛuman ssiliman seg tqucac u deg yiḍ timeẓrit a aydeg ufan assebɣes meɣɣer
imi ay yennires maṛyus nezzeh belli acengu atan yezlen yenẓed iten ad gen tasusmi talqayant
yessegdel ula d acuffu deg lebwag am deg wayen iɛeddan micki sneflen taganit n yiḍ akked tafrara
deg tegnit aydeg ṛmin yicenga uzzren deg yiḍen
s teẓwayt s lɣila yenẓed imḍafen d wid yeḍḍfen lbuqat deg tgalufin d trebbuyaɛ ad suḍen meṛṛa ɣef tikkelt i yiserdasen ad suɣen s uɛeyyeḍ n yimenɣi d wenṭag beṛṛa i teqcelt
kkren d leɛyaḍ a yejtulen d yimuriṭaniyen yesrebriben war ma zemren ad rewlen wala ad ddmen imrigen wala d gen kra
dderz asuɣu tibawt n tallalt timduggin timyeḍfarin n yiserdasen nneɣ lxelɛa aya akk yeɣmer iten deg tiddehcert yuẓen ɣer yisiḍ
deg tgara ddirzen u rewlen yillaf d yemrigen nsen ttwaḥellan d deg ttergigin seg llan beḍḍun iḍ ɣef kuẓ n tiɛezziṛin n yimuren tagara n yal aḥric tettwaberraḥ s usuḍu deg lbuq u llan sskaren taḍaft n yiḍ yinḍafen n yiḍ yettwasmeskalen s temlellit kuẓ n tikkwal
tuget nsen
amḍan n wid yemmenɣen deg tinnuɣi a yugar ayen yemmenɣen deg tmennuɣin yezrin akk
acku iḍes yeswawi d arebrab yeswa tarewla nsen
seg s akkin ineyyer ikemmel maṛyus abrid is ɣer tegrest ay yeɣtes ad tt yeǧǧ deg temdinin tiftisin akken ad yelmeḍ useddur ɣas akken tarennawt ines ur as d teswawi ara tawzizt wala tizzengert
ur yettemhaz ara arma yessuleɣ amkuẓ am wakken sdat n ucengu
sula yetteddu d yemnayen deg yiri ayeffus ɣef uzelmaḍ inyus manilyus ay d yemekkaten n yillan d ayt ikuffa deg tgalufin tiliqurin
deg tazwara d tagara yessebded inezzurfa d iserdasen akk ifessasen iserdasen imaynuten ayɣef ulac attkal aṭas yerna ur ssinen ara nezzeh tamurt ttganin tikli n ucengu daɣ aqenṣul am wakken ulac ula d yiwen i tallalt is
netta yella yettageẓ yalec
yella yemmegnet deg yal adɣar yessedgir s yiwar n warur asmineg d uzawar yezga yettwarbeb yemmuteg ur yesḍulli iserdasen s waya
yezga yuki ɣef taggazt n tikli n yiserdasen kifkif deg wayen yerzan asselɣet n teqcelt asgen
yuzen i taḍaft n tewwura tigalufin tiṛumaniyin u sdat n teqcelt n yemnayen imaragen yessers nnig waya ammasen niḍen n yiweẓla n usselɣet nnig weḥfir
d netta s timmad is ay yettagen agawes mačči d tugdi ay yugad ur ttwasselkamen ara yenziḍen ines maca yebɣa ad iẓer iserdasen ines ttdeggin iweẓla a aydeg tettekka yid sen
daɣ netta deg tallit a n yimenɣi mgal yugurten kifkif am yumenɣiyen niḍen yemmesten maṛyus ɣef weɣyud deg yigen s uḥulfu s userhu ugar tugdi deg tmernut
mačči d yiwen ay yerran aya ɣer tzitla
wiyaḍ qqaren dakken yennum seg temẓi tudert tagermamt yella yestumun s wayen umi qqaren lmertat tiggucert akken yebɣu yili tewwi d seg s tegduda abɣur am wakken ay t id tewwi seg yal tanbaḍt ay yesɛan ugar n wanɣud
lḥaṣul deg tgara n wass wis kuẓ ur yeggug ara ɣef qerṭa uɣalen d yifaḍaḍen s lemɣawla seg yal tamiwin ɣef tikkelt ttberriḥen d s tilawt n ucengu maca imi seg yal tamiwin ay d wwin isali yiwen ur yeẓri ara aqenṣul d acu n uɣawas ara yeg i yimenɣi
yeɣtes tagara ur yesmeskil acemma deg uɣawas n tikli is ara yessurfen s tririt n yal tamdigt
yesqudd s ugani deg waddad aydeg yella
yugurten ay yellan yebḍa igen ines ɣef kuẓ n yikeffulenn yunẓa dakken yiwen n ukefful seg kuẓ ad ideg acengu sdeffir maca ayenni yebrer sula yemmuger anegges amezwaru n ucengu anda imnayen ines ay yebḍa d tigulaf yemlalen yemmeẓyaren u fell asent ay neṭgen yinumidiyen u yeqq usuger n yigen yessinif aɣelluy n yikuffa ay d yettwakalen seg wuggug
yenɣa akk wid ay d yuẓen ɣur s lawan n yimenɣi n yemnayen yenṭeg d buxus ɣef tdeffert nneɣ s yiterrasen ay as d yewwi mmi s wulux imenɣi ay as d yewwi mmi s wulux ur nettsekka ara deg tinnuɣt yezrin imi ay yennugra deg webrid
yella maṛyus imir nni deg tezwert anda ay yella yugurten s timmad is yessedday imedru
mi slan yinumidiyen s wawwaḍ n buxus yuɣal mebla ma yella win ay t yeẓran din isuɣ s taɣect timinegt s tutlayt talatinit ay yessen deg ussutel n numans belli tinnuɣi teṛjeḥ i ṛṛuman u belli tura kan ay yenɣa maṛyus s ufus is imir nni ibeyyen d agestur is yumes d idammen n yiterrasen nneɣ ay yenɣa s tebɣest deg tinnuɣi
s tmesliwt n wawalen a ḥulfan yiserdasen nneɣ sdat tizudt n waya ḥulfan s wexlaɛ ccil assurdu ay asen yeqqar yemsiwel
aya yessuli tabɣest lberber ay iẓedmen s wemsad ɣef ṛṛuman umi yeɣli waddur ay iheyyan ad rewlen imi ay yerna sula imenzaɣen
idegga ɣef yifer n yimuriṭaniyen imir nni kan yeddirez buxus
ma d yugurten isegger ineḍfaren ines i wehras n trennawt ay d yuzen ad d tettwaḥelli
maca yettwassutel s yemnayen u yeẓra akk ineḍfaren is ɣlin ɣef yeffes zelmeḍ yuhez iman is ɣer sdat u yessemres ad yelli asaka talemmast n yesmuden n ucengu deg tegnit aydeg yuzzel maṛyus deffir imi ay yerra imnayen n ucengu ay yeẓra la d tteddun ɣer terẓi
ifuk yalec s truẓi tamatut n yinumidiyen timeẓrit tessexlaɛ s teɣzi n teɣzut tallunt tarewla timenɣiwt assekref irgazen tilawin igmar ẓẓlen deg lqaɛa meṛṛa dlen s waggasen ur zmiren la ad rewlen wala ad thennir ttarmen ad bedden ttuɣalen ɣellin dindin lḥaṣul deg yal adeg teɣzi n tmuɣli lqaɛa tella
tdel s yemsuden s tzibawin tifekkiwin deg yibellaɛen n yidammen
deffir tedyanin a ay asen yesnekden tarennawt aydeg ulac assurdu tikkelt a yewweḍ uqenṣul ɣer qirṭa
iswi n tikli seg tazwara da deffir kuẓ n wussan segmi ay rrẓen lberber wis sin n yiberdan usan d yimazanen seg buxus ttettren t s yisem n ugellid ad as yazen sin n yergazen aydeg yesɛa taflest i umsiwel yid sen ɣef teɣdeft ines netta d tin n wegdud aṛumani
yuzen maṛyus imir nni kan lukyus sula d inyus manilus ay iɣetsen akken ad ddmen awal ula ma usan d s tinnubga n ugellid akken ad t id sduddcen ɣer yiḥulfan ufrinen ima haqel ɣur s tidmi n userrase n terbabt yerna ma yebɣa tamazzalt
sula umi yeǧǧa manilus awal ula ma wesser i lmend n tasraqqa ines
yessenfali d s tewzel s wawalen a s yimisi a agellid buxus s tumert d tameqrant i nekkni ara nẓer irebbiwen tagara ad gen tamhergit i wergaz am kečč akken ad yessemyif tamazzalt ɣef yumenɣi u belli agellid ummid am kečč ad yeḥbes ur yessamas ara iseɣ ines s umyawaḍ d bu tinɣiwin yugaren akk wiyaḍ yugurten u ad tessunfed fell aneɣ taḍullit n tmernut inek ɣef yideg n tinnuɣi a ay iweɛṛen i usguccel s tseddi wali gsell asuneḍ asebter
taɣzut tullint ayɣef ay d yettmeslay salustyus tezzel arma d deffir n wasif n lɛutmaneyya ahat deg temnaḍt n celɣum lɛid ma yeggug ugar n wayen nezmer ad nurdu dakken maṛyus ahat yekka d ɣef tefrawt n cclef
sakkin beṛwageyya d ṣur lɣezlan
deffir mi yedd tama n wezrar n biban iɛedda ɣef usayes n meǧǧana
am wakken ara nessufger tedra ines abekkaḍ ines
rnu agdud aṛumani seg tamenzut yella yesmenyaf ad yesɛu imidawen wala aklan
yefles yumen ugar ad yessebded tanbaḍt ines ɣef leḥmala mačči ɣef tdusi
ɣef wayen ay k yerzan kečč ulac tamidawit ara k yesbeɣren yifen tamidawit nneɣ d tamezwarut acku neggug s wayen ad tenkeẓ tmeẓla gar aneɣ daɣ netta ad aɣ tessuref ad ak nefken tawalin s timmad nsent am wakken ay nemyadas
rnu ɣas ur aɣ nkiẓen ara yimidawen d yineḍfaren nekkni wala imidawen nneɣ yiwen ur yesɛi agdaz
tanemmirt i yiṛebbiyen imi seg wass amenzu ay teẓram tifrat a
tellam tzemrem ad d tḥellim ɣer wegdud aṛumani gar n teɣdeft wala aganed aydeg tellid
maca artum d netta ay yesseddayen tiɣawsiwin n tallsa yebɣa ad k yerr turmed s nnuba tadusi d umuzzu nneɣ
imir a imi ay ak tettunefk tlemmiẓt ɣiwel semmed ayen tebɣid yagi tilemmiẓin ur k usarent ara i wakken s leqdic ik n tura ad teddud agulen inek yezrin tagara sɛun taflest deg waya agdud aṛumani ur yestehzay ara ɣef tukci n tulluɣt usar
ma d azal is aserdasi aql ik teẓrid t seg llina
yerra d buxus s wawalen imadkaten d imidawen yerna asen kra n wawalen i tmastant ma yeddem tarbabt ayen mačči d alekkid mgal ṛṛuman maca i ummesten ɣef tgelda ines acku amur seg numidya ayseg ay d yettwaẓẓeɛ yugurten yeqqel d ayla is s wezref n weslak u belli ur yeẓẓider ara ad tt iẓer tettwandel s ufus n maṛyus nnig waya yella yuzen sin n yimazanen ɣer ṛuma yetter tamidawit nneɣ ayen ur as yettwadeggan ara maca ur yettḥettit ara ɣef yimezri
ma yessuref maṛyus netta yenmuteg ad yazen tagensest tura kan ɣer useqqamu n yemɣaren simi tettef tanaḍt yesmeskel uberbari amnad ines s weswar n yimidawen sɣur yugurten ay ines yettwaggufsen yugaden deg wayen yettwasxudsen deffir mi yeẓra s tizziwt n sula d manilyus
yuɣ lḥal deffir ma yessers igen ines deg tsegrest ines yewwi yid s iterrasen fessusen d kra n yemnayen iṛuḥ ad yessutel tiɣremt tageldant deg wenẓul anda ay iga yugurten tamastant seg yiserdasen imerwalen imir nni yesmeskel buxus amnad ines tikkelt niḍen ya yesnezgem ɣef wayen ay as d swawint snat n tinnuɣin ay iɛeddan ya ad yili yeḍfer isemtaren ay as fkan yinesɣamuyen ines ay as d yeggran ur ten yesguffes ara yugurten
yefren buxus semmus n yimidawen ines umi yessen timmekdit d tigzi yesseɣlef iten s ṛṛwaḥ ɣer maṛyus sakkin ɣer ṛuma ma idegga yefka asen akk tinnezgit ad mmestagen ad as ɣetsen ɣef tammazalt ṛuḥen i semmus ɣer tegrest n ṛṛuman maca ttwassutlen deg webrid ur ttwakren seg yigezzamen n webrid i ur neẓri acemma am wa ay neẓra
yugurten iṛeggem i buxus s umur deg numidya ma yella ttwaẓẓɛen ṛṛuman neɣ ifuk yimenɣi s wezlaɣ n tlisa ines
leḥmala
cennɛen ijituliyen u netlen ɣer sula ay yeǧǧa uqenṣul u netta iṛuḥ deg temdukt s wudem n
ttergigin deg yiwen n waddad ahlilif yemmuger iten id sula mačči am yicenga yebbuḍren am wakken uklalen maca s waṭas n lemkabra yesban d tanakkaft armi ay ɣilen yiberbariyen a belli temɣer n uɛebbuḍ ayyes ttwassnen yiṛumaniyen d agul u belli sula d amidaw nsen imi ay yesseṛwa asen isefkan acku aṭas n medden ur ssinen ara imir nni taẓuri n taɣin n yifraken
ttɣilen belli kra n win ay yellan d anakkaf ur yetteg ayen ala s tulluɣt u yal asefk yettussemḍen d tagga tizziwt ayyes n ttwasmeglen u ssutren seg s tamastant d asemter u sseknen tadusi d takdit d tanemɣurt n ugellid nsen s tewzel yal ibɣuren ay ssarmen yiṛumaniyen ad tent iṛeggem asen sula s wayen akk ssutren u yemla asen amek ay yessefk ad as mmeslayen i maṛyus sdat n useqqamu n yemɣaren
sakkin ggunin ɣer s tasmakta n kuẓet n wussan
yuɣal d maṛyus ɣer qirṭa deffir yessemda taḍugt is u yesla s wawwaḍ n yigensasen umi ay d yessawel seg ɛutiqa akked sula u yeẓra d daɣ i lebruṭur lukyus i usnejbar s ur aɣ d yenni ara uqbel dakken ɛutiqa d yiwet seg tsegrit
yenna d kan dakken maṛyus yesker taqcelt ines deg temdinin tiflisin i ussenked d usselmed n umeddur ay yettwagza seg waya dakken maṛyus yeddirez seg numidya s wudem aneggaru
billinus
deg tegnit a dɣa yal amaslaḍ yella deg tfesna n yemɣaren ay yellan deg friqiya yessisen as meṛṛa ɣef tikkelt s yisumar n buxus
yessuref uqenṣul i yigensasen ad ṛuḥen ɣer ṛuma
ssutren wi tarekkiḥt deg tegnit n westag
tettunefk asen s udegg n sula d ticcemt
kra sbanen d taɣert n waddud ttun war assurdu tammaskalt n tɣawsiwin n tmeṭṭi d temlellit nnes timmezgit deffir mi ttwadeggan yissutren n yimuriṭaniyen ɣdan kraḍ deg sen ɣer ṛuma akked usefrak kinyus uktabyus rusin ay d yusan ɣer friqiya s tiɣraḍ n yigen uɣalen sin niḍen ɣer ugellid ay yeḍḍfen s waṭas n tumert assemres n tgensest nsen ladɣa arettu d uclaɛ ay asen yefka sula deg ṛuma deffir mi gganin yigensasen a aseqqamu n yemɣaren ad yessuref ɣef wagul ayɣer yeɣli ugellid nsen s tikerras n yugurten
ssutren sakkin tameqqunt d tamidawit nneɣ u yerra asen d s yimeslayen a aseqqamu n yemɣaren d tulluɣin wala wegdud aṛumani ur tibekkadin maca imi buxus yemmugreẓ ɣef wagul is ad as nessuref
ma d tamaqqant n wemsasa d timmidawit ad as tettunefk asmi ara tt yuklal
deffir mi yegza s tririt a yura buxus i maṛyus yessuter seg s ad as yazen sula d amastag i tifrat n wakk tiɣawsiwin ay ten yerzan
iṛuḥ uneggaru a akked taḍaft n yemnayen d yitarrasen d yimakkaten n yillan lbiyar rnu imakkaten n yemsuden d tgaluft
ttettun ara la seg imrigen n yemsersanen iwakken ad izmiren ad teddun s leɣawla di tegnitt i deg yettmestan fell asen akken iqudd seg yemsuden n ucengu maca seg wass wis smus n tikli ẓṛan s tuẓwayt deg usayes amellun waluskus mmi s n buxus ulac yid s nnig n wagim n yemnayen maca imi llan leḥḥun war aɣyud u bruzzɛen banen d isula d yemdukal is i yellan ugaden sen temdugt icenga belli amdan nsen ugar
diɣenna yal yiwen yella yessenɣad amrig is u yessitib iman is mmutgen i yimenɣi ma d tuggdin ur banent ara diɣenna asirem ur iba ara ima ara d mmektin tirennawin d ḥellan mgal acengu agi s timmad is
di tegnit agi dɣa uɣalen d yemnayen yettwaznen i waggay n isalen ɣef taɣult
nnan d belli yalec yerked akken dɣa i yella lḥal
imi d yewweḍ walus yezzul ɣef imsefrek u yenna yas belli baba s d netta i t id yuznen i temlilit is yak d tdukli yid s
ddan akken ass amezwaru d win ɣer s war amihi
tameddit imi gerwen deg teqcelt yuzzel umuritani ɣer sula iwakken ad as yini belli ifadaden ssisnen as tura kan belli yugurten ur yeggug ara timatarin n lxulɛa banent d ɣef wudem is
yettḥettit fell as iwakken ad faṛṣen iḍ i trewla s tuffra netta yid s
yerra as d sula s tfenzayt belli ur yettagad ara anumidi agi ẓẓṛan t aṛṛuman acḥal n tikelt u belli yesɛa taflest temmed deg iserdasen ines
ulamma ad immet war asurdu ad yeqqim wala ad trewla igad yettneyyiren wala anadi ɣef yekneḍ
yesfugguyen
d asenǧem n tudert ahat teggunitt tmettant s waṭas d yuẓen imi t yessemter ugeldun s usikel inhed xeṛttum deg yiḍ yettef amnad agi din din iserdasen ad faken učči s lemɣawla d usiɣi n wayen iwumi zemren n times deg teqcelt d usikel zzeg s akin
deg uddekki deg uɛeẓẓer amezwaru tura ɣer tessarmi ten tikli n yiḍ
yella sula yesɣawas i tideg n teqcelt ima ara d yali yiṭij imir dɣa ssisnen as d yemnayen imuritaniyen belli yugurten atan iga tiqcelt ines ɣer usurif n sin imyilen ɣer zdat xelɛen iserdasen nneɣ imi slan i usali agi ɣillen belli waluks ikneḍ itenu belli ɣlin deg ukmimalammi kra suɣen s usuter n tiɣawt u ssutren i wakken ur yettɛedday ara wenkaḍ agi war tamernut
ulamma sula yella yettḥulfu am nitni maca issegdel askar n kra n tekriḍt mgal imuritaniyen
issedger inedfaren ines ad sɛun tabɣest amagnu ad nnaɣen ayagi iɛeddan kra n yebɣasen mgal igen d anemɣur w ad hellin tarennawt u belli skud ttḥezziben drus skud ttilin di tɣellist ugar
u belli d ixiḍ imi ara lili terbaɛt ger ifassen ad yili uɣiwel i netta ur yerbib ara u ad nerr amihi s tuzzya n tfekka nneɣur nẓeṛṛ ara ur nettarra ara tiyitwin i wcengu
deffir wayenni iseggayet amenɣur ɣef ubekkaḍ d tkerras n buxus
inkeḍ walux ad yeffeɣ di teqcelt imi yennizeḍ am ucengu
aneggaru agi iḥellel it s imeṭṭawen i wakken ur yesseflas ara taɣawsa am tagi ur llint tkerras deg way agi yakmaca ilmend n tiḥerci n yugurten i wumi ssisnen ifadaden ines belli ṛṛuman la ttagen tikli nsen nnig wayenni yunẓa belli ur yezmir ad yeg acemma ɛinaniimi ulac ɣur s ala igen d ameẓyan ladɣa s tihawt d tmeẓṛiwt n mmi s n ugellid i ɣef yessebded yakk anaruz d umeddur ines
ihi am akken iẓeṛṛ yif it ad iɛeddi s tebɣest di tlemmast n teqcelt is deg wayen t irzan netta yella walux yemmuteg ad yazen
imuritaniyen ines ɣer zdat neɣ ad ten yeǧǧ ɣer deffir d tiɣimit iman is idd sula ilmend n waddad yettwaṭṭef usumer agi u kkunesren din din slemẓen taremmuyt d ukukru d iswawi waggaḍ nsen aẓwayan ur yugurten d uɛddi war tasiweɣt
zzeg s akin s kra n wussan wwḍen taggara n usikel nsen
yella imir nni deg yeɣrem n buxus yiwen unumidi itedder yid s qqaren as asbar yuzen it yugurten simi yegza s tasin n sula i ugenses ines d tamagaẓt n tidmiwin ines n umsasa ines diɣen am akken yella diɣen dabar mmi s n suqrada seg twacult n massinisa maca seg marwa tanafsast seg tama n tsettit
ilul d bab s seg tmeṭṭut tuffirt swawit as d tuẓulin leḥmala d tanureft n ugellid
yella yesban d deg waṭas n imaɣlayen takdit ines i ṛuma
yuzen it buxus s lemɣawla iwakken ad yessisen sula belli yemmuteg ad yesselkem tinbaḍin n wegdud aṛumani yessuklef kan ɣef sula ad yefren s yiman is ass d yideg d tamert n wemsiwel nsen
war taremmiɣt seg ugensas n yugurten u belli ur isemmeskel ara assaɣen ines netta d uneggaru agi s unegmer iwakken ad yizmir i westag s tlelli ugar ɣef teɣdaf igerwen
acku ulac kra n wallal nniḍen i usinef n tkennaḍ
nekk s timmad iw mennedleɣ belli ulac kra yellan d adetti di tfakulin d issentel buxus u belli s tidmi n diri yeṭṭef yejgugel deg tmazzalt d tnumidit deg yiwet n tegnitt u belli aṭas i yenna deg wallaɣ is ma da gella ad ifek yugurten i ṛṛuman neɣ ad ifek sula i yugurten
rran t id ɣer teɣdeft nneɣ
yerra d sula belli ad yili
ihi d awezzlan nezzeh deg umeslay is zdat asbar
ayen d iqqim ad ilin fell asent yemsawalen uffiren idd agellid inigan neɣ zdat wemdan d ameẓyan
di tegnit nni s timmad is izzubbet d tiririt i yebɣa ad a t id tuɣal
tella temlilit akken yebɣa yenna belli yettwazen d s ɣur aqensul iwakken ad iẓeṛ ma agellid yebɣa tammazalt neɣ imenɣi
imir nni yunez ugellid i teknutin i d yewwḍen
iḥellel it ad yuɣal di mraw n wussan u belli ur yeɣtis acemma ar tura maca ad d yefk tiririt ines imir nni
zzeg s akin msebḍan tidmi n diri iqertaǧiyen ur sɛin la talɣunt wala alɣun di tɣawsa agi maca tanfalit agi tuɣal d anza deffir imenɣi abuniqi d anamek ɣef tedmi n diri
yuɣal yal yiwen ɣer teqcelt is
deg yiḍ yeɣra d ugellid i sula s tuffra tummidt ur yelli yelli yid sen slid at tsuqqelt d at teflest yak d babar i yettaflasen sin idisan am abdammas yeddem ugellid awal din din ur d yusi ara deg yixef iw werǧin nekkini s yiman iw unnig n igelliden umadal agi d anemɣur n igelliden yakk
ssneɣ ad d yass wass ad iliɣ deg s ttwalaseɣ s ɣur amdan d amagnu ad ggalleɣ a sula belli ullaleɣ aṭas n madden zdat ma wer k ssineɣ
kra s uḥellel seg sen kra s tleffut war ma usareɣ yiwen
tura ur sɛiɣ ara aglam am wagi
wiyaḍ ttnuɣnin ttmendayeɣ s wemyagal ttḥulfuɣ s tumert ad iliɣ usareɣ asuter n timidawit ik am tɣawsa i zennfen ɣer wul iw
tesɛiḍ afran ad termiḍ agella inu
imrigen idrimen s yiwen wawal ayen yezzubẓen ad t tessirmeḍ awi t ddem it eg yes s ayen i ak yehwan skud teddreḍ ur ssuḍin ara belli rriɣ areṭṭal tussnaw n tnafut ik ad teqqim tezga di talqa n wul iw akken bɣun ilin iseddiren inek ad d afen astan ɣur i skud ddreɣ acku di tedmi w yif it ad yettwarnu ugellid deg imenɣi wala ad yettwarnu di tnakkaft deg wayen yerzan tiɣawsiwin n tegduda nwen i ɣef uznen k id ad ten tefruḍ dagi s yisem ik d asemmagul
irgazen asemmagul i win d anamek anesḍuf yettwakellfen ad yedbel lemluk n win meẓẓiyen neɣ anerzam neɣ anabay ssin akin qqaren t i win yettuɣellfen ad yesseddu tiziwt s yisem n uwanek
ttaken t hatayen wayen riɣ ad t id iniɣ kra n wawalen ur skireɣ ara ur bɣiɣ werǧin ad sekreɣ imenɣi mgal agdud aṛumani
mmestaneɣ kan s terbabt ɣef tlisa i d uzɣen s terbabt
ad uɣaleɣ deg teɣtast ma tebɣam ay agi
nnaɣet d yugurten akken i wen yehwa ur zeggreɣ ara asif n malawiya i yettwasmersen zik nni d tilisa gar i d makibsa ur ssurufeɣ ara usar i yugurten ad a t yezger
ma yella kra tesɛiḍ ad t id tessutreḍ nniḍen dg i u ad at tuklaleḍ u ad t yuklal wegdud ik ur tettṛḥuḍ ara bla ma tḥellaḍ t
sula ɣef wayen i t yerzan netta s timmad isyerra d s tewzel tameqqrant u s waṭas n tmanzalt maca yesseɣzef aṭas ɣef tmanzalt d iɣudfin yezdin ur yeffir ara ɣef ugellid belli aseqqamu n yemɣaren d wegdud aṛumani deffir mi t rnan s terbabt ur ssemnaḍen ara ireggimen imagnuyen d tiwriqin n wakaz i nitni
yessefk ad as yettwafek wanza akmam ɣef waqqas amaleɣ ines ara yesbeɣren ayagi d ayen ilemḍen imi d yugurten gar ifassen is
ma yefka t i ṛṛuman ad ilin yettalas asen areṭṭal u ad as fken s tleffut tamidawit d tamsist yakk d umur n numidya i yessuter ass agi
yugi ugellid di tazwara u yeṭṭef deg wawal is
tafakut is d tiḍḍgla yak d ugatu yettwazemlen gar asen gar as d yugurten rnu ɣer wayagi yugad ma yeẓṛa tamaqqant agi ad fell as wgad yettɛuzzun yugurten annect uksanen ṛṛuman taggara di ṭṭaqa uḥettet rewlen tidwas ines yengugin yermin seg iban d yunez ugar
ireggem ad yeg ayen yakk yebɣa sula mtawan ɣef iselkamen ara yessenẓen yugurten s udeggi n weɣtas ɣef tammazalt i t yerran
imenɣi yuqem yessaram ay agi s unafag
ssuddsen taxazabit akkgi umsebḍan
azakka nni yeɣra ugellid i asbar agensas n yugurten u yenna yas d belli sula yessisen as d ɣef brid n dabar belli yeẓẓubeẓ ad yettwaseḥbes imenɣi s tewtilin i ɣef ara yili udiwenni
yetter it ihi ad iẓeṛ tidmi n ugellid is
iṛuḥ asbar s tdawit tameqqrant ɣer teqcelt n yugurten
yewwi yal iwellihen sakin yeddem abrid is s lemɣawla yuɣal d deg wass wis ṭam ɣer buxus u yessisen as yugurten ad idegg akk ayen yettwasutren deg s maca yessurda maryus
acḥal n tikelt i qqnen nitni d inabbaden n ṛṛuman timsasayin u qqiment mebla aselkem
ma yebɣa buxus ad yageẓ iɣdafen nsen imezdiyen u ad yessenked tammazalt tadettit yessefk fell as ad yessuddes s tfakult n tmazzalt agraw ad iɣer i yigad yak terza tɣawsa imir nni ad as dyefk sula imi ara yẓeṛ useqqamu n yemɣaren d wegdud aṛumani udem n texxutra am tagi ddaw tanbaḍt is ur yessewzizen ara deg tuqqna n tifratur ttaǧǧan ara udem bab n waddur am wagi ddaw ufus n ucengu d tegzemt mačči n wazdal mačči n tekdit ines i tegduda
deffir mi ywemmem umuritan s telqayt yewweḍ ɣer uṛeggem ahaqell aglugel ines yella d asulu neɣ d tidet ur neẓṛi ara nnit rnu tiɣtasin n igelliden s umata d timugdaz maca ttilint diɣenna d tuḍrinin u ttemyagalent tikwal
akken yebɣu yili yettwasbedd wakud d yideg n wegraw
yella buxus tikwal ad iɣer i sula u tikwal nniḍen i ugensas n yugurten yettmagar iten s tmidawit
yettak i yal yiwen ireggimen yemmegdan i sin llan ččuṛen d anaruz d tadawit iḍ yezwaren ass n temlilit yeɣra d umuritani i yemwaziyen ines ssin akin yessetti amnad ines s tuẓwayt u yessuter ad ffɣen bih bih
aṭas n wemsiwel i yellan itezzi deg yixef is
yella wudem is d wallen is
ttemṣeṛɣant d iḥulfan yellan s timmad nsen zzizine t u ttcenniɛen taggara uffiren itettin deg yixef ines xas ma yessusem taggara yeɣra i sula mtawan ad gen akmin i yinumidiyen
s akin di tafrara imi as ssusnen s tazin n yugurten yuhez buxus ddan yid s kra n yemdukal yak d imsefrek nneɣ wmager ines amzun ad a t sserhun bedden ɣef yiwet ntiɣilt ẓeṛṛen ten id igad yettwaɣelfen ad gen akmin gganin t yella unumidi yeddukel d d waṭas iɛeggalen n ugurad is
usan d diɣen war tarbabt am akken mtawan yagi
simi yettwafka usiɣel yettwasutel si yal tamiwin seg yigad igan akmin nni
akk wigad yeddan yid s ttwanɣan netta yettwafka deffir mi yettwaqqen i sula i t yewwin ɣur maryus
di tegnitt nni simi wwin d inabbaḍen nneɣ kantus d kibyus manilyus wwin d tiṛṛẓi zdat iɣaliyen
ayen d iglan s lxulɛa di yal iṭalya
deg wass n ar tura mmenzin ṛṛuman balli ma igduden meṛṛa ad anzen s ussigel zzat tebɣest nsen ma d nitni d iɣaliyen yella imenɣi mačči ilmend n tminegt maca ilmend n tudert akken diɣenna imi slan di ṛuma belli imenɣi n numidya ikfa d waggaḍ n yugurten ɣer temdint yettwaqqen
rran d maryus s tefranin d aqensul
ccil n tibawt ines yettwaɣlef ɣef temnaḍt n ɣala
yesfugel s trennawt is s wefcar d ameqqran di kalanda di uktuber aseggas yeṛṛeẓ uqensul kinyus malinus libruqensul kintus sirfilyus kibyus deg tinnuɣi idi n uranǧ meɛna tiṛṛẓi n uraǧ mačči zdat niɣaliyen i d teḍra am akken i d yeqqaṛ salustyus meɛna zdat ikenbariyen
ttwanɣan di tinnuɣi agi tamet n igiman n iṛumaniyen
tamentilt n tiṛṛẓi d tuggut n manilyus ad yuhez iwakken ad d ifek afus n tallelt i kibyun
urfan meqqrit di ṛuma alammi yettwakkes kibyun seg tizwitin ines
awal n iba yexxiter acku asaḍuf yessefk tihawt umankaḍ ɣer tqensult s timmad is di ṛuma lawan n tefranin i tikelt tamezwarut yella werkaḍ usaḍuf di taɣult agi
am akken ara naf azlay nniḍen ɣef usaḍuf i d yettbanen deg wallas n wefran n maryus i tikelt tis snat mseḍfarent ulamma asaḍuf ur yessuruf ara s wallas n wefran n uɣerman i yebɣu yili t i twuri n uqenṣul
slid deffir mraw iseggasen ɣef tefrant tamezwarut
yennayer deg imir fell as i semman iɣallen d inaruzen n temdint
